    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c4ade749-7a10-4ceb-930d-1f236f377f52'

  <span id="freeText17703068732602161459" style="display:none"><b>He knows how to score, on and off the ice</b><br /><br />Allie Hayes is in crisis mode. With graduation looming, she still doesn’t have the first clue about what she’s going to do after college. To make matters worse, she’s nursing a broken heart thanks to the end of her longtime relationship. Wild rebound sex is definitely not the solution to her problems, but gorgeous hockey star Dean Di Laurentis is impossible to resist. Just once, though, because even if her future is uncertain, it sure as heck won’t include the king of one-night stands.<br /><br /><b>It’ll take more than flashy moves to win her over</b><br /><br />Dean always gets what he wants. Girls, grades, girls, recognition, girls…he’s a ladies man, all right, and he’s yet to meet a woman who’s immune to his charms. Until Allie. For one night, the feisty blonde rocked his entire world—and now she wants to be friends? Nope. It’s not over until he says it’s over. Dean is in full-on pursuit, but when life-rocking changes strike, he starts to wonder if maybe it’s time to stop focusing on scoring…and shoot for love.</span>

<div id="review_1440218378" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1440218378" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1440218378?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1440218378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12244021144406040760"><b>5 stars!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/FE6FD941-4F3E-4D91-A737-F383949B4957_zpsvav51bjc.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451556208i/17558156._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo FE6FD941-4F3E-4D91-A737-F383949B4957_zpsvav51bjc.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It’s very rare that I read a series with 3 books and all 3 are equally fantastic and solid 5+ star reads for me. When starting <i>The Score</i> I was a little nervous it wouldn't live up to all the hype. I loved the first two books in this series so hard, I could only hope this was as good. I think <i>The Mistake</i> is still my favorite because, well… Logan. But honestly, this was just as good as <i>The Deal</i> for me and solid 5 star read! <br/><br/>Dean and Allie are two characters we’ve known and loved since</span>
  <span id="freeText12244021144406040760" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/FE6FD941-4F3E-4D91-A737-F383949B4957_zpsvav51bjc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451556208i/17558156._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo FE6FD941-4F3E-4D91-A737-F383949B4957_zpsvav51bjc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s very rare that I read a series with 3 books and all 3 are equally fantastic and solid 5+ star reads for me. When starting <i>The Score</i> I was a little nervous it wouldn't live up to all the hype. I loved the first two books in this series so hard, I could only hope this was as good. I think <i>The Mistake</i> is still my favorite because, well… Logan. But honestly, this was just as good as <i>The Deal</i> for me and solid 5 star read! <br><br>Dean and Allie are two characters we’ve known and loved since book one. I was so anxious to see how Dean would be in this book… how does the ultimate college man-whore settle down? Is it even possible one woman could make him fall? Maybe… just maybe if it’s the right girl. And they have the right chemistry. And she can keep him on his toes. And just maybe this girl won’t want anything to do with Dean Di Laurentis after one night. But we all know she’d only be fooling herself. Because it’s DEAN! Dean has a life motto for christ’s sake! I just adore him. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I do what I want, when I want. And I don’t give a shit what people think about me.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/55925037-DE17-460B-83C8-3BEB8862ED07_zpss9z9szha.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451556209i/17558157._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 55925037-DE17-460B-83C8-3BEB8862ED07_zpss9z9szha.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me just say there is a lot more to Dean than what meets the eye. I love the Elle gives her characters this depth you wouldn’t expect. I didn’t think there would be so much to Dean, but there absolutely was. And Allie was pretty fantastic as well. I loved how she didn’t easily give into Dean and his ways like all the other girls on campus seem to. I love me a feisty heroine! Dean met his match when he found himself wanting her. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/D7327C09-C01C-4314-BA41-264BBF7D254E_zpstmlidjuh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451556209i/17558158._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo D7327C09-C01C-4314-BA41-264BBF7D254E_zpstmlidjuh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is so much I love about these stories, but really I think my absolute favorite thing is the bromance between these guys. The four friends that live in this hockey house together are loyal, they have each others backs, and they are seriously a complete hoot when they’re together. I can’t even tell you how many hilarious lines between Dean and Garrett, Logan or Tuck that I highlighted! <br><br>This is one of the best new adult series I’ve ever read. When it comes to college romances, this one takes the cake. Seriously. If you haven’t read them, stop what you’re doing, and pick up <i>The Deal</i> right this minute. Elle Kennedy will give you love, laugh out loud humor and amazing off the charts chemistry. Her characters are lovable and these books are just fun to read with the perfect amount of feels and emotions. <i>The Score</i> goes on my must read list! This is one I highly recommend! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I thought you said you didn’t want to… And Dean Di Laurentis only does what he wants, remember?”<br><br> “I am doing what I want. I’m making you happy.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/81D1029B-4DC8-4F12-B894-F59251C0701E_zpspzpgxykw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451556209i/17558159._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 81D1029B-4DC8-4F12-B894-F59251C0701E_zpspzpgxykw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267516555?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14262653-mysza?shelf=favorite-read">favorite-read</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267516555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16838004571806426170"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450702300i/17458058._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, I’ll be damned! I loved The Deal and didn’t think it would be possible to top it, but The Score, OMG! The Score was even better!!! The best part in the series! So yeah, I guess it’s time for Snoopy and the happy dance. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450702300ra/17458059.gif' width='400' height='250' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Nothing about the plot from me because I encourage you to read it yourself, but I promise, you will laugh and get teary-eyed and get all mushy inside. All because of Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis. Holy shit, this guy is swoonworthy. Really, I’m in love, so bac</span>
  <span id="freeText16838004571806426170" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450702300i/17458058._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, I’ll be damned! I loved The Deal and didn’t think it would be possible to top it, but The Score, OMG! The Score was even better!!! The best part in the series! So yeah, I guess it’s time for Snoopy and the happy dance. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450702300ra/17458059.gif" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nothing about the plot from me because I encourage you to read it yourself, but I promise, you will laugh and get teary-eyed and get all mushy inside. All because of Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis. Holy shit, this guy is swoonworthy. Really, I’m in love, so back off ladies, Dean is mine. Let me count the reasons:<br>1. Doesn’t like to wear a shirt, like ever.<br>2. Is dirty in bed, with a power to seduce with just words that spill out of his mouth. <br>3. Reformed manwhore. Yeah yeah, you know the type, we all love them. But once he gets Allie, he is loyal, so no worries about hanky panky on the side ladies.<br>4. Boy is smart, like really smart with good grades and all. Who would have thought, huh? <br>5. Is also super funny and cheery most of the time. The banter and sweet talk between him and Allie is awesome.<br>6. And finally, he will squeeze out of you all those warm feelings. You. Will. Fall. Head. Over. Hills. In. Love with HIM.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450702300ra/17458060.gif" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Dean isn’t the only great thing that makes this book wonderful, Allie as a heroine is kickass too, plot is fabulous and I loved catching up with the whole bunch. Truly, it was fantastic, mark your calendars for January 11th 2016. You don’t want to miss this book, I swear.<br><br>Now, only Tucker left, and judging from that last sentence…. his book might be… interesting. So yeah, keep that shit up Elle Kennedy because you are doing a fine job. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421962574ra/13436591.gif" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16838004571806426170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1267812956" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1267812956" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267812956?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267812956" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15496605831769270453">The funniest, most irreverent and emotional book in the series by far. My friends know how much I loved The Deal, and I love it still. I really do but this book...gah! This book made me laugh and it also made me cry. Yes, cried because apparently, Elle Kennedy had a few surprises up her sleeves which totally broke my heart.<br/><br/>The Score is the third book from Kennedy's wildly popular NA sports romance series, Off Campus. This time, the story centers on Dean, the unapologetic and self-proclaimed manw</span>
  <span id="freeText15496605831769270453" style="display:none">The funniest, most irreverent and emotional book in the series by far. My friends know how much I loved The Deal, and I love it still. I really do but this book...gah! This book made me laugh and it also made me cry. Yes, cried because apparently, Elle Kennedy had a few surprises up her sleeves which totally broke my heart.<br><br>The Score is the third book from Kennedy's wildly popular NA sports romance series, Off Campus. This time, the story centers on Dean, the unapologetic and self-proclaimed manwhore of the team. Dean has had it easy. He's good-looking, rich and doesn't lack for any female or male adulation. But Dean's life became a lot more interesting when Allie Hayes, Hannah's best friend, came to stay over at their house one night to avoid her ex-boyfriend who want to get back with her. Dean being Dean, he put on the moves on Allie despite warnings from Hannah and Garrett.<br><br>Unfortunately, Allie was unimpressed. She knows Dean's reputation and she doesn't want to be just another notch on her bedpost. She knows who she is: a girl who is prefers relationship over casual sex. And Dean is the epitome of casual. Besides, Allie just broke up with her on-and-off boyfriend of three years. But Dean was persistent and he managed to convince Allie to ditch her no casual sex rule in favor of some hot rebound sexy times.<br><br>I personally cannot blame Allie for capitulating because when Dean wants something, he is tenacious and he can turn on that Di-Laurentis charm like nobody's business. Allie didn't stand a chance. Heck, I didn't stand a chance. I was swept right along with Allie.<br><br>I love reading this aspect of the book. We all know by now that Elle Kennedy is a master at banter, and that's never been more apparent than in this book. I could not contain my chuckles and my grins while reading. My husband had to shush me because I could not hold my laughter in. It's simply impossible not to laugh at some of the things that happened or at some of the dialogue in this book. I thought The Deal and the Mistake were funny, but the Score took it to the next level because Dean was a natural comedian. Same with Allie, too. She can go toe to toe with Dean with no problem at all.<br><br>I know there were a few readers who were disappointed that Sabrina wasn't the heroine for Dean but let me tell right now, I'm not sorry it wasn't Sabrina because Allie totally owned my heart from the get go. She's feisty, funny and like I said, she's unimpressed with Dean and she made him work for it. Dean and Allie simply worked together. Sure, Allie had her moments of guilt and indecision but the author explained those very well I sympathized with her. I knew where she was coming from and I could understand why she would feel that way.<br><br>But the best thing about this book is how you get to see Dean and Allie fall for each other. It's so rare to read a book that actually shows the hero and heroine fall for one another in a series of moments instead of just being told that they are in love. There's no insta-love here. NONE. And I LOVED that because even though Dean and Allie were physically intimate with each other and are crazy attracted to each other, they didn't fall in love immediately. It took time for them to fully trust one another. But the moment they did, oh man, it was well worth the wait. Seriously, Elle Kennedy should conduct a workshop on this non-insta love thing because I much prefer my romance like that.<br><br>Apart from the romance, there were other layers to this story. We see Dean change and grow as a character. We read about Allie deal with her limited career choices. We see the gang worry about life beyond college, about whether or not they're going to still be friends with each other or lose touch. Dean and Allie also had to deal with disappointments and tragedy. There were so many things in this book that rang true for me based on my own experiences in college.<br><br>I also loved that there were no slut-shaming in the book. My usual complain about NA and sometimes with contemporary romance is that when you have a manwhore hero, we usually get the whole "all the other girls are sluts except the heroine and her friends" shtick. The characters had to own up or gets called out on heir prejudice about sex and hook ups, and it's perfect. I could not hate Dean or feel bad for the girls who chose to have sex with him simply because they were written as characters with agency. And there were some things from Dean's past that should've raised my hackles, usually, but it didn't because again, Elle Kennedy treated it with sensitivity and it worked perfectly with Dean's character arc.<br><br>I really can't find anything to complain about this book. I finished it with a huge smile on face because it met all my expectations, and I hope it will meet yours, too!<br><br>I refrained from posting some quotes because you guys should experience all the funnies yourself. And trust me, if you loved the previous books in the series, you will undoubtedly love this one as well. <br><br><br><i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br>_____________<br><br><br><br><b>Dean's book??</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/o86KGVA" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394806986ra/8908636.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/bQFVgst" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386254222ra/7322574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15496605831769270453" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1269121694" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1269121694" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1269121694?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-alpha-hero">favorite-alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=humorous-reads">humorous-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=keeper-shelf">keeper-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=steamy-romance">steamy-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1269121694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7334364081969008559"><b>5 Stars</b><br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450659539r/17452974.jpg?v=1450659542368' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I kiss him back hungrily, helpless to resist him. Dean Di Laurentis is in my blood now. I didn't expect this intense sexual chemistry between us, but it's here, and it's addictive, and I don't know how I can ever give it up.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450737086ra/17461603.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>You know when you read the first book in a series and you love it so much that you don't think anything can top it, but then you read the second and you love it just as much? So then you know that the chances of that continue to hold for the 3rd book are sl</span>
  <span id="freeText7334364081969008559" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars</b><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450659539r/17452974.jpg?v=1450659542368" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I kiss him back hungrily, helpless to resist him. Dean Di Laurentis is in my blood now. I didn't expect this intense sexual chemistry between us, but it's here, and it's addictive, and I don't know how I can ever give it up.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450737086ra/17461603.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You know when you read the first book in a series and you love it so much that you don't think anything can top it, but then you read the second and you love it just as much? So then you know that the chances of that continue to hold for the 3rd book are slim, right? In my experience, it's tough to keep that sort of momentum going...unless, of course, you're Elle Kennedy. Because not only was The Score absolutely fantastic, but it turned out to be my favorite in the series. And considering how much I loved the previous two books, that's saying something.<br><br>Now let's be real here; considering how much I love me my manwhores, it was already a good chance I'd love Dean Di Laurentis. Even the man's name is hot, for goodness sake. Between his self assured ways, cocky attitude, humor, and manwhoring tendencies, I couldn't get enough of him.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">The guy has the attention span of a fruit fly, and the affection-giving habits of a puppy, offering his sexual devotion to whoever happens to be holding the treat. By which I mean the vagina.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450737086ra/17461604.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What I love about Elle's writing, is the depth that she gives her characters. And Dean certainly was no exception. He may be the hard partying manwhore with a crass sense of humor, but beneath that perfect exterior there's so much more to him and you really get to see it blossom here.<br><br>Allie Hayes is Hanna's best friend that just recently broke up with her long term boyfriend of 3 years. In fear of giving in when he comes calling again, Allie seeks an escape at Garrett's place. She knows all about Dean and his one and done ways and he may be hot but he's not for her. She's a nester. She has relationships not one night stands. But then a broken heart and some tequila lead to one of the hottest hookups of her life with none other than the sexy manwhore. She's determined to keep it in just friends zone after but Dean is determined to change her mind.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Have you considered seeing a psychiatrist about your delusions?" I ask politely. "Because, sweetie, there's no chance in hell of us boning tonight."<br>"Fine. How about we go down on each other instead?"<br>"How about you leave?"<br>"Counter offer- I stay and we dry hump."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The Score is this amazing combination of witty humor and endearing characters. While I loved the slow building romance between Dean and Allie, what kept me turning the pages was the banter between them and the rest of the guys. The Twilight references alone had me laughing like a loon. It was witty and crass, and wildly entertaining. Dean and Allie together was the perfect examples of opposites attracting and I absolutely loved them together. Their banter and chemistry was utterly delicious.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">...last I checked, genitals don't decide who gets to listen to their music first."<br>"Oh yes, they do...<br>See, if you take away my dick privileges, I'll be fine for moths. Years, even. But if I take away your pussy privileges? You'll be utterly lost. Like a drowning man at sea, desperately grabbing for the vagina preserver. Therefore, vagina trumps penis."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved how Miss Kennedy pulled off an incredibly sexy romance while keeping it realistically slow paced. These two may burn up the sheets together, but the feelings came with time and I for one loved watching those develop for both of them.<br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450736672r/17461571.jpg?v=1450736675303" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This isn't just a story of the manwhore meeting his match and inevitably succumbing to his feelings for her; it's so much more. The story had wit and humor and so much depth to it, too. There's something that happens towards the end that caught me completely off guard. I never in a million years expected something like that to happen and yet as much as it broke my heart, I can't help but to admit it did the job of driving the plot where it needed to go.<br><br>Without a doubt, Elle Kennedy is a force to be reckoned with. The woman can write the hell out of a book. Dean and Allie's story was funny, sexy, swoony, emotional and wildly entertaining. It was everything I love about romance and exactly why I read New Adult. THIS is how it needs to be done. I can't wait to see what the next book brings, because after that little peak we got? Oh yeah! It's about to get real.<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>Find me on:<br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/DirtyGirlRomance?" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525717.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow me on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/DirtyGrlRomance" target="twitter" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525718.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow Me on Twitter" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="http://www.dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525719.png" width="40" height="40" alt="blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267703335" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3476763032682341896"><b>*****4.5 STARS*****</b><br/>{ARC Generously Provided by Author in Exchange For an Honest Review}<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/9de3a3bc50a9026681cc6c61ce206827_zpshln2oim3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451277542i/17524265._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 9de3a3bc50a9026681cc6c61ce206827_zpshln2oim3.jpg' width='365' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Elle Kennedy definitely has another HIT on her hands with this one. The <i>OFF CAMPUS</i> series delivers the <b>HOTTEST</b> Hockey Players, panty melting scenes, and laugh out loud moments as well. Each guy is pretty cocky and gorgeous, but never do they come off as narcissistic pricks.<br/><br/><br/><br/>Dean Di Laurentis is a serious <b>PLAYER</b>. He enjoys sex and is a serious exhibitionist as well. He also doesn’t have any desire to be in a</span>
  <span id="freeText3476763032682341896" style="display:none"><b>*****4.5 STARS*****</b><br>{ARC Generously Provided by Author in Exchange For an Honest Review}<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/9de3a3bc50a9026681cc6c61ce206827_zpshln2oim3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451277542i/17524265._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9de3a3bc50a9026681cc6c61ce206827_zpshln2oim3.jpg" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Elle Kennedy definitely has another HIT on her hands with this one. The <i>OFF CAMPUS</i> series delivers the <b>HOTTEST</b> Hockey Players, panty melting scenes, and laugh out loud moments as well. Each guy is pretty cocky and gorgeous, but never do they come off as narcissistic pricks.<br><br><br><br>Dean Di Laurentis is a serious <b>PLAYER</b>. He enjoys sex and is a serious exhibitionist as well. He also doesn’t have any desire to be in a serious relationship with any woman and he always makes his intentions clear with every girl he hooks up with. The one time he attempted to be in a relationship ended disastrously and several years later he is still haunted by the past.<br><br><br><br>Allie Hayes is Hannah’s best friend and roommate. Hannah is Garrett’s girlfriend and I’m sure none of you have forgotten <i>THE DEAL</i>. That book was on my top ten of 2015 list. Allie has just broken up with her boyfriend of the past three years and is feeling vulnerable. She wants a clean break from him but he isn’t willing to give up on her. So in order to avoid her ex, she spends the night at Garrett’s house, where as luck would have it, Dean happens to be.<br><br><br><br>Allie knows Dean and is fully aware of his reputation, which makes her immune to his charms. She isn’t like any of the girls he hooks up with. But after several shots of tequila and a couple of puffs from a joint, Allie finds herself waking up the next morning naked in Dean’s room, with a serious hangover, and a gloriously naked Dean as well.<br><br><br><br>The sex turned out to be mind-blowing for the both of them and after a ton of resistance from Allie, the two enter into an arrangement. They agree to have sex on a regular basis and to not see other people while doing so. But as they start to spend more time together, feelings begin to develop and pretty soon they question whether there might be something more than just sex between them.<br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/686eceb26e74266209d3c08e01241c66_zpsro01jcr9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451277542i/17524266._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 686eceb26e74266209d3c08e01241c66_zpsro01jcr9.jpg" width="363" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>We learn how life has been pretty unfair to Allie and how things aren’t always what they seem where Dean is concerned. He lets people think he’s just a pretty face with a limited vocabulary, but he’s destined for Harvard Law and it’s due to his academic prowess and not his family’s bank account. I found myself comparing Dean to Grayson from <i>The Friend Zone</i>, which only made him that much more lovable to me.<br><br><br><br>There were some angst filled moments, but they were quickly resolved and I wished that they had been drawn out just a bit longer. Expect to laugh your ass off at least a few times, especially during the bath tub scene with Winston. The steamy scenes were seriously freaking <b>HAWT</b>!! Dean is pretty insatiable and I guarantee that you will either be taking a few cold showers, attacking your man, or spending some quality time with your Winstons.<br><br><br><br>This book releases on Jan 11th and I know you’re all going to fall in love with this story and Dean!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/16094605_zps20no7cph.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1472174557" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1472174557" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1472174557?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1472174557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13473108158748281321"><b>FIVE MAN WHORE STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Maybe it’s time to stop focusing on scoring…and shoot for love.</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452380673i/17687075._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series has well and truly got me wrapped around its little finger. If I could reproduce the feelings I have when reading one of the books in this particular series, then my happiness levels would be set for life. Talk about sweeping me off my feet, this hero has gone and made himself my favourite out of all Elle Kennedy's boys; no small feat let me tell you, this author has a particularly wonderful talen</span>
  <span id="freeText13473108158748281321" style="display:none"><b>FIVE MAN WHORE STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Maybe it’s time to stop focusing on scoring…and shoot for love.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452380673i/17687075._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series has well and truly got me wrapped around its little finger. If I could reproduce the feelings I have when reading one of the books in this particular series, then my happiness levels would be set for life. Talk about sweeping me off my feet, this hero has gone and made himself my favourite out of all Elle Kennedy's boys; no small feat let me tell you, this author has a particularly wonderful talent of making her men irresistible. 'The score' is not to be missed, forgotten or side stepped. In fact all romance readers (who haven't yet had the fortune to 'meet' these characters) should make it their quest to read them immediately. Trust me you won't look back. <br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>After her latest heartbreak, Allie Hayes decides to make a personal pledge to avoid making the same mistakes again. Allie will do anything and everything to avoid getting her heart involved. Setting out to concentrate on making her dreams a reality she has no interest when the possibility of a one night stand with the notorious man whore, Dean Di - Laurentis becomes a possibility. But after one drink too many and with an itch to scratch, Allie lets her hair down for just one night. But after getting just a little taste of the sassy blonde Dean finds himself wanting more. And so begins the cat and mouse chase of a lifetime ... This hero wants Allie all for himself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452380673i/17687076._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>Every. Single. Moment. There was not a word, sentence or chapter that didn't have me glued to the action. The romance was on point, the characters were adorably addictive and the story line had me hooked. But over everything else this book made me laugh like no other in the series, the banter was on point and the connection and friendship between the characters was one that I don't think I'll ever forget about. Elle Kennedy really does have an incredibly special talent at making me fall in love with her words and you would have be insane if you didn't find something to love about this reformed man whore and his sassy counterpart. Plenty of emotion, scorching hot chemistry and a romance story that had me feeling all the feels. I really can't find fault with this diamond of a book and it's official the off campus series is crowned as one of my all time favourites. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452380673i/17687077._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>There should not be a single romance reading addict left on the planet who hasn't started this series. I'm being deadly serious, it's a crime against the romance reading world to have not experienced this authors insane ability to create a new adult romance of epic proportions. If you are one of those readers (yes, I'm looking at you) who has not yet got themselves wrapped up in this gorgeous series then I whole heartedly recommend that you stop right where you are and Start. It. Now. And as for me well I can sit back with the biggest smile on my face after meeting a hero that quite frankly will be taking up residence in my book heart for a long time to come. However, i'm more than happy to make room for more from Elle Kennedy if she's going to keep up this standard of hero worship. Readers, I adored Dean and Allie their story is adorable, soul searching and one to not miss out on. I can't wait for my fellow romance addicts to fall in love like I have. Enjoy ... Kisses. <br><br><b>
  <i>*ARC provided in exchange for an honest review.*</i>
</b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267814844?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A." href="/user/show/22324639-a">A.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=liked-it">liked-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=athletes-fighters-n-such">athletes-fighters-n-such</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267814844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10770695270938270760"><b>ANOTHER WINNER!!!</b><br/><br/>I adore this series and I loved this book, I really did. Dean is my favorite in this series. The book contains all the elements I love in the college romance genre: a manwhore-turned-prince-charming hero, a strong and determined heroine and lots of steamy and LOL moments. <br/><br/>So why not 5 stars?<br/><br/>Allie and Dean’s relationship seems a little superficial. Their relationship is based on sex and watching soap operas. Don’t get me wrong, they really are a perfect match, but I didn’t really</span>
  <span id="freeText10770695270938270760" style="display:none"><b>ANOTHER WINNER!!!</b><br /><br />I adore this series and I loved this book, I really did. Dean is my favorite in this series. The book contains all the elements I love in the college romance genre: a manwhore-turned-prince-charming hero, a strong and determined heroine and lots of steamy and LOL moments. <br /><br />So why not 5 stars?<br /><br />Allie and Dean’s relationship seems a little superficial. Their relationship is based on sex and watching soap operas. Don’t get me wrong, they really are a perfect match, but I didn’t really feel their love. And although the author is trying to portray their relationship as a slow-building one, it still seems rushed to me. <br /><br />I had a problem with the flow of the story too. The beginning and the end of the book are flawless but I got bored around the middle of the book.<br /><br />I also caught myself rolling my eyes a few times, for instance during the tomato scene which seemed immature and unrealistic.<br /><br />But those are only minor flaws. I still think that this book is a must read and I can’t wait for Tucker’s story!</span>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1471950444?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-sports">cont-sports</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1471950444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2750098229759166116"><b>Can a manwhore recover from manwhoritis?</b><br/><br/>I started <i>The Score</i> on my birthday. Happy Birthday to me!!!! The sucky thing about my birthday is that it’s a week before Christmas. I’m celebrating with my friends and family with a little voice inside my head saying “would these people hurry up and eat their cake…<i>The Score</i> is waiting”. Now I did say I was celebrating, which did involve wine. So by the time the friends did leave, the night time rituals had been done and I’m finally ready to crack <i>The Scor</i></span>
  <span id="freeText2750098229759166116" style="display:none"><b>Can a manwhore recover from manwhoritis?</b><br><br>I started <i>The Score</i> on my birthday. Happy Birthday to me!!!! The sucky thing about my birthday is that it’s a week before Christmas. I’m celebrating with my friends and family with a little voice inside my head saying “would these people hurry up and eat their cake…<i>The Score</i> is waiting”. Now I did say I was celebrating, which did involve wine. So by the time the friends did leave, the night time rituals had been done and I’m finally ready to crack <i>The Score</i> open…I’m tuckered out. I think I got two pages read. It’s OK, I woke up early and got reading straight away…then another birthday party intruded…and a Christmas party…and another Christmas party. <i>The Score</i> was being neglected, but it was definitely not forgotten. All of these things slowed down my progress. I’d managed to get to 77%, loving it, needing it and wanting it, when it all came to an abrupt stop. I GOT FOOD POISONING!!! I’m literally dying and my first thoughts in recovery…”My birthday present…<i>The Score</i>…Why…Why…Why did this have to happen to me?” A little melodramatic, but I was really llloooppyy. <br><br>Oh well, can’t help the loopy, but I HAVE FINALLY FINISHED IT!!! It took a week, but I’m so glad I did wait. That last part packed a punch and I needed to be whole and hearty to <i>Deal</i> with it and all <i>The Mistakes</i> that could have cost Dean <i>The Score</i>. Maybe I’m not over the loopy just yet ;)<br><br>The story starts out with Allie breaking up with her long time boyfriend Sean. She loved him…or so she thought, but would someone who loves you want to change you? Sean’s plans for their future did not include her following her dreams to become an actress. His plans were for them both to return to <b>HIS</b> hometown, where <b>HE</b> would join <b>HIS</b> father in business and <b>SHE</b> would become the little homemaker. Pffft…tell him his dreaming. Luckily she woke up to herself and realised their dreams were different. Unfortunately, she’s used to being in relationships and loves the comfort of having a partner. She must remind herself to stay strong against his <i>Sweet Attacks</i>, because she’s fallen for them before. Her best way to avoid an attack, is to avoid him. Easier said than done and she must bring in Hannah, her best friend, to help guard and reinforce her barriers. Hannah’s solution is for Allie to stay at her boyfriend Garrett’s house. All those ice hockey heroes can protect her.<br><br>Dean Di Laurentis, <i>Manwhore Extraordinaire</i> is having a "sandwich". He’s the filling and the two blonde chicks are the bread. Now this is not Dean’s first "sandwich", but it sure is putting this Friday night in his “best night ever” folder. Things are heating up when the doorbell rings. His plans get shot to smithereens when babysitting duties are forced upon him. His buddy’s girlfriend’s friend needs a place to hide out…and there goes his "sandwich".<br><br>From the very beginning Dean’s character surprised me. We know him as the manwhore who gets off getting off with numerous women on the couch in the lounge room. But the guy had absolutely no hesitation on chucking out the "sandwich" and going hungry. Dean was a very different character to the one I’d imagined. It didn’t take me long to jump in the “Dean is Awesome” fan group.<br><br>Allie’s NOT looking for a relationship and who would be silly enough to think that Dean would be relationship material? She wants to concentrate on her career in acting, and look after her father who has an incurable disease. But Dean has magical boy bits and she can’t resist. Soon they come to a mutual understanding that they’ll hook up for awhile. They spend time together outside of the bedroom and Allie can’t help but join the “Dean is Awesome” fan group. Funny thing is, Dean can’t help but start an “Allie Rocks My World” fan group too.<br><br>The journey for Allie and Dean is far from smooth. Besides their relationship, there are things with their career paths, families, friends and lifestyles that need to be dealt with. They’re young and still don’t have all of the necessary experience to handle everything thrown at them, but I was impressed that they learnt from their mistakes and managed to move on from them. They don’t take the easy route and they also accept the consequences of their decisions. What seemed like an easy life for Dean, soon becomes hard. At first he struggles, but when push comes to shove, his intelligence, upbringing and education help him to work through the difficulties.<br><br>I really enjoyed this story and loved seeing the maturity blossom in both Allie and Dean. Can a manwhore recover from manwhoritis? In Dean’s case, I’m not sure he was sick from it. I do think that he had an opportunity to enjoy his good looks and privileged life to the absolute full and took it. He didn’t plan for it to be his life and with his upbringing and loving family as a great example of what life was all about, knew there were more important things in his future.<br><br>Elle Kennedy, <i>The Score</i> was another win for me. I cannot wait to see what comes from Tuck’s announcement. Oh boy, oh boy, oh boy….<br><br><b>I received a complimentary copy of this story via the author for an honest review.</b><br><br>To buy <i>The Score</i> from Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1klc7W8">http://amzn.to/1klc7W8</a><br><br><b>I’m an Aussie chick who loves to read and review romance, drink coffee, be a <i>Style Setter</i> and stalk David Gandy. To see more of my reviews, fashion, food and pervathons -</b><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447925695i/17069306.jpg" width="170" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br> <br></span>

<div id="review_1267792142" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1267792142" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267792142?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Elle Kennedy Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267792142" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12301115958668702723"><b>5 The Life of Dean Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>As a huge, massive, seriously devoted fan of <b>The Deal by Elle Kennedy</b>, I was over the top thrilled to see the success of her new series Off-Campus. I enjoyed reading about people in college who had dreams and goals; who experienced things in their lives which shaped who they were and when confronted with real challenges, pulled from within... muscled through...coming out the other end, better. <br/><br/>These books had humor, drama, amazing sexy times and most</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12301115958668702723" style="display:none"><b>5 The Life of Dean Stars<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>As a huge, massive, seriously devoted fan of <b>The Deal by Elle Kennedy</b>, I was over the top thrilled to see the success of her new series Off-Campus. I enjoyed reading about people in college who had dreams and goals; who experienced things in their lives which shaped who they were and when confronted with real challenges, pulled from within... muscled through...coming out the other end, better. <br><br>These books had humor, drama, amazing sexy times and most of all, none of the over the top angst so many other stories can have. As someone who doesn't read the angsty, heartbreaking type... this was a series made just for me and others who felt the same way.</b><br><br>Well, people.... This does not disappoint. This brings us back to Briar College and the troops. We are right where we need to be to watch Dean Di-Laurentis meet his match. We are privy to Dean's and Allie's POV's and being in their heads gives us all of the feels we need. <br><br>Now I know all of you are wanting to now about Dean... the man who invented the perfect Dick Shot... yes, the one which instructed his friends to hide the balls... because let's face it... balls are not sexy. <br><br>Yes, that Dean is there in all his sexual glory... the flirt, the one track mind, the man who loves to party with all the willing women... and know... there are willing Twins, duets and all sorts who wish to experience the Dean...and in the past books, Dean was more than happy to oblige. His one hardcore rule was everyone had to be on the same page... meaning...a clear understanding of what the hook up was- fun and games... no relationship.<br><br>And that is the Dean we catch up with, the man who has the happy existence. He does what he wants, is with who he wants and lives to the fullest.<br><br>He lives in a house full of his hockey teammates. Two of them have met their women and are in bliss. Hannah, Garrett's girl has brought a balance to his friend and she has fit in with all of them. It is her best friend Allie who becomes a thorn in Dean's side at first.<br><br>For Allie has finally pulled the plug on her long term on again off again relationship with Sean. They started in her freshman year with the understanding of what would happen at the end of college... the both of them going off to do what they had planned...She to pursue her passion in acting... him, off to Vermont to work at his father's insurance company. What developed was a push pull between them; Sean trying to manipulate Allie to being "the little woman supporting her man" syndrome.<br>He wanted her to give up her dreams; never admitting she was worthy of all the success she had had... for she had been acting since a child. This wasn't some pipe dream... she had done plays, commercials and was with an agent who was booking her for a possible Fox series. She was fully in the game...and Sean just discounted her and finally said all the things needed for her to see clearly- it needed to be over.<br><br>Allie called Hannah and asked if she could help her. She had told Sean it was over and he was non stop texting and saying he was coming to her dorm. Hannah arranged for Allie to stay at the house... only problem is Hannah won't be there with Garrett... only Tucker and Dean will be there. Hannah has Garrett text the guys to let Allie stay and then Garrett separately texts Dean to lay the law down about Allie. He is to keep his dick in his pants... he is to stay clear of her. Allie is given the go ahead to stay at the house for the weekend.<br><br>Dean was rather occupied when the text about Allie was sent... so he had no clue anyone was coming over, let alone Hannah's bestie. Dean was in a trance of mystical proportions...instead of 2 of everything... there were 4...He was living the dream all guys have when wanting more than what one person can give...He was about to enter nirvana when the banging on his door interrupted his entering the treasured path....<br><br>There at the door was Allie with a backpack and suitcase. As Dean looks at her in his boxers, no shirt...he is confused as to why she is here and starts to tell her she missed Hannah as they have left. Allie states she is here for the weekend As he tries to close the door to have his playmates get dressed, Allie walks in, plops down on a chair and says, Carry on... don't let me bother you...<br><br>Well, that kind of ruined Dean's mojo...and all of the parties leave with Dean promising a rain check. Annoyed but curious, Dean asks what is up. Allie explains the situation and hands Dean her phone. He is to stop her from reading Sean's texts or her using it to call him. He is her break up sponsor for the weekend. <br><br>Dean takes all of this in and actually is understanding...yet also does his "Dean" thing of suggesting he help her through it by having sex with him. Allie looks at him as if he has 3 heads... She would never be with him...she is a relationship gal... not into casual sex... never worked for her...and Dean has banged half of Briar College and the other half is just waiting to be chosen... oh, no... not happening.<br><br>Allie set up Netflix and insists on picking the movie. Somehow she wins and Dean is stuck watching some flick about a woman dying of cancer. As the movie progresses, Allie refuses to admit it sucks...Dean decides there is only one way to continue watching...Tequila.<br><br>I don't think I need to tell you what happens next....<br><br>Allie wakes up and she is not in a bed alone...her hangover is so bad she can hardly see...but what she does see is a sleeping vision of glorified man. ...naked...and all of the flashbacks coming rushing to her head....<br><br>This cannot be happening...but it did and now what. Dean stirs and Allie is caught with his eyes on her....There is teasing from him but also concern...a pact is reached;<br>They will never talk about this again. <br><b>It Did Not Happen</b><br>For the sake of all that is holy, both know Hannah and Garrett and all the others cannot know so they are on agreement. She leaves to stay with another friend and that should be that. <br><br>But it isn't. Because Dean had the best experience ever with Allie...and he can't understand why he is only interested in her. Other women are coming on to him and his usually friendly other half... known as Little Dean, is just not responding. This has never happened... like ever. After three days, he reaches out to Allie and tells her he wants to have a repeat... she shuts that down. <br><br>There is so much more to this story than just the start of this relationship. We find out why Dean has acted the way he has and his growth arc is done with slight of hand and then leaps and bounds. Allie has been on a serious path for very long time. She had a family which loved and cared for her, experienced what it was like to lose a loved one and now is devoted to her father. With his management of MS becoming harder and harder, Allie has made decisions based on it. She has been a caretaker for a very long time, not always doing what is best for her or allowing others to do for her.<br><br>We are with these two as they find away to each other. We see them separately as they figure out their own needs for growth, career and love. These two at first would seem like a wrong combination because Dean has only shown the side he thinks other want to see. In this we are gifted with the reveal of the actual man he is. <br><br>Oh, he isn't perfect by any means and when he falls, he falls hard... but he is loyal and true. He doesn't take and not give. He has the intelligence to see clearly when something needs to be addressed and when able, does. <br><br>Allie is this woman who has many sides to her... and she is learning all about them through Dean. Their times are playful, incredibly hot and both of them rejoice in the couplings. The way they tease and text is perfection. It is terrific to experience a woman coming into her own sexually and not feel guilty while doing it. While there may be moments of insecurity; overall, Allie is strong and capable in who she is, what she wants and where she needs to be to achieve her goals. She is very like able. <br><br>This book took me on a journey with characters I had bonded with from the start. Elle Kennedy gave me <b>The Deal</b> with the foundation of these people and then she built a second floor with <b>The Mistake</b>...a strong and solid read in keeping with the same architectural style... of humor, open sexuality and heart. With <b>The Score</b> she has added another level to an intricate structure. It reflects the time just before people go out into the world and leave the shelter of college. It gives us insight to what these specific characters need to grow and see who they are going to become...it presents challenges and then these characters either rise to carry on or don't. <br><br>Elle Kennedy has somehow made these difficult years something we want to continue experiencing through her characters. They are not perfect but damn they are fun. I know the next installment will bring even more challenges to the forefront and I can't wait to see how Ms. Kennedy handles it.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1431282052s/24920901.jpg" alt="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>The Deal (Off-Campus, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1201019883">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564665.The_Mistake__Off_Campus___2_" title="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1447598937s/25564665.jpg" alt="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1213223269">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27252717.The_Score__Off_Campus___3_" title="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1493326480s/27252717.jpg" alt="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Score (Off-Campus, #3)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1267792142">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28262024.The_Goal__Off_Campus___4_" title="The Goal (Off-Campus, #4) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1477069102s/28262024.jpg" alt="The Goal (Off-Campus, #4) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Goal (Off-Campus, #4)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1506928328">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></b><br><b>~~~~~ Before Reading ~~~~~</b><br><b>
  <i> The skies opened up...<br>My prayers were answered....<br><br>Dean, I'm coming for you...<br><br>If you don't hear from me for awhile...<br>Know Dean and I are checking out the accuracy of those Dick Pics he sent me....</i>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7120092382414046273"><b>HOT DAMN! LOVED IT!</b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>THE DATING GAME questions with Dean and Allie: </b>
</u><br/><b>1.</b> I’VE HEARD YOU ARE PERFECT, DEAN. IS THERE ANY TRUTH TO THESE RUMORS?<br/><b>”Yeah. I am perfect. I need to remind myself of that more often.”</b> <br/><br/> <b>2.</b> ALLIE, PRIOR TO GETTING TO KNOW DEAN WHAT WAS YOUR IMPRESSION OF HIM? <br/><b>”If I’m being honest, I’ve never known what to make of the guy. He’s cocky, flirtatious… Superficial.”</b> <br/><br/><b>3.</b> COULD YOU SEE YOURSELF GETTING TOGETHER WITH HIM?<br/><b>”He’s annoying and ridiculous and totally not my type.”</b><br/><br/><b>4.</b> DEAN,</span>
  <span id="freeText7120092382414046273" style="display:none"><b>HOT DAMN! LOVED IT!</b><br><br><u>
  <b>THE DATING GAME questions with Dean and Allie: </b>
</u><br><b>1.</b> I’VE HEARD YOU ARE PERFECT, DEAN. IS THERE ANY TRUTH TO THESE RUMORS?<br><b>”Yeah. I am perfect. I need to remind myself of that more often.”</b> <br><br> <b>2.</b> ALLIE, PRIOR TO GETTING TO KNOW DEAN WHAT WAS YOUR IMPRESSION OF HIM? <br><b>”If I’m being honest, I’ve never known what to make of the guy. He’s cocky, flirtatious… Superficial.”</b> <br><br><b>3.</b> COULD YOU SEE YOURSELF GETTING TOGETHER WITH HIM?<br><b>”He’s annoying and ridiculous and totally not my type.”</b><br><br><b>4.</b> DEAN, YOU GIVE ALLIE SOME ADVICE ON HOW TO HANDLE HER BREAK-UP WITH HER EX. WHAT WAS THIS GREAT WISDOM YOU SHARED WITH HER?<br><b>”The best way to get over someone is to hook up with someone else. ASAP. Seriously, just find yourself a rebound. I volunteer as tribute.”</b><br><br><b>5.</b> One last thing, Dean, how do you feel about shirts?<br><b>”I don’t like shirts.”</b> <br><br>Now that you’ve gotten to know Dean and Allie a little better have fun reading about them in THE SCORE. I love this series and, at the moment, this book is my favorite of the series. I was sucked in by everything that makes a college romance good - the drama, the love-hate relationship, manwhores, relationship girls and jealousy. I loved when Allie would get stuck in her head she’d quickly realize she was over analyzing the situation and pull herself out of her “mental talk”. A lot of times the female characters can be annoying with the inner dialogue and Allie did a great job of catching herself in those moments and turning the inner babble off. The Score was just the right combo of all things that make NA genre entertaining. <br><br>The Score is my third book by Ms. Kennedy and after that ending I’m anticipating the next book in the series. <br><br>TO READ<br> <b>Garrett &amp; Hannah’s</b> interview -&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1227744913">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br>and <br><b>Logan &amp; Grace’s</b> interview -&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1255727116">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><br>✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦<br><b>RELEASE DATE: 1/11/2016</b><br>Pre-order | order: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1Qw2UbP">http://amzn.to/1Qw2UbP</a><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564665.The_Mistake__Off_Campus___2_" title="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1447598937s/25564665.jpg" alt="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer11489839203294440928"><b>3.5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>Really need half stars here Goodreads. The fact that there was skimming involved warrants a rounding down, BUT there were some pretty damn funny lines that make me want to round up. <br/><br/>Honestly, for me this felt like a repeat of book 1 and 2, just changing up the main characters names. <br/><br/>Seems like all of the men are reformed manwhores (really really over it), the couples want to keep their proclivities on the DL, and the hero does something stupid at the end. No? <br/><br/>I know I'm in the minority</span>
  <span id="freeText11489839203294440928" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars!</b><br /><br />Really need half stars here Goodreads. The fact that there was skimming involved warrants a rounding down, BUT there were some pretty damn funny lines that make me want to round up. <br /><br />Honestly, for me this felt like a repeat of book 1 and 2, just changing up the main characters names. <br /><br />Seems like all of the men are reformed manwhores (really really over it), the couples want to keep their proclivities on the DL, and the hero does something stupid at the end. No? <br /><br />I know I'm in the minority...I expected to be. <br /><br />I liked Dean and Allie fine. I just can't say anything about the story really wowed me. Other than the last paragraph of the book. Well played there Elle! <br /><br />I wasn't a huge fan of the plot device used to create the conflict but it didn't annoy me <i>too</i> bad. <br /><br />It was entertaining enough, certainly funny, relatively low angst and pretty damn hot. <br /><br /><b>

<div id="review_1286769863" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1286769863?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
