        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1286769863" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15940483207943699355">First things first, can we take a moment to appreciate the <b>gorgeousness of this cover?</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424291678ra/13740894.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Second, if I can't have a John Logan (because Logan will always be my number one hockey hottie) <b>can I have a Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis?</b> <br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413895019ra/11577801.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And third, <b>is there a way to stop drooling?</b><br/>(No? I thought so.)<br/><br/>I am a bad, <i>bad</i> girl. I have a shitload of work to do, I have the most brutal exams of my life approaching but do I study? Hell no, I just fall in love with the hottest athletes that an author has</span>
  <span id="freeText15940483207943699355" style="display:none">First things first, can we take a moment to appreciate the <b>gorgeousness of this cover?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424291678ra/13740894.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Second, if I can't have a John Logan (because Logan will always be my number one hockey hottie) <b>can I have a Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis?</b> <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413895019ra/11577801.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And third, <b>is there a way to stop drooling?</b><br>(No? I thought so.)<br><br>I am a bad, <i>bad</i> girl. I have a shitload of work to do, I have the most brutal exams of my life approaching but do I study? Hell no, I just fall in love with the hottest athletes that an author has ever created. <b>I need help. </b>Seriously guys, I'm open to suggestions, interventions or therapists' numbers. I'll accept any offer that will pull my mind out of the gutter, even though I'm afraid I'll need an extension ladder and a generous dose of bleach to scrub my dirty thoughts. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454602256ra/17990449.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Seriously, just find yourself a rebound.” Dean whips up his arm. “I volunteer as tribute.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27252717.The_Score__Off_Campus___3_" title="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Score</a> we're dealing with a <b>friends-with-benefits-that-fall-in-love</b> situation (which explains the graphic-and sometimes <u>extravagant</u>-sex scenes) between Allie, a girl who just broke up with her longterm boyfriend, and the infamous man-slut/ horndog/ sex addict Dean. There is chase, tention, sneaking out and eventually emotions, heartbreak and problems that will affect their relationship, but Dean imprinted on Allie and he will not let her go. Sounds like a fun ride, right?<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The guy has the attention span of a fruit fly, and the affection-giving habbits of a puppy, offering his sexual devotion to whoever happens to be holding the treat. By which I mean the vagina.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27252717.The_Score__Off_Campus___3_" title="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Score</a> was great, but in my opinion <b>not as funny and cute as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564665.The_Mistake__Off_Campus___2_" title="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mistake</a></b>. Don't get me wrong, I still enjoyed it very much, and <b>I swooned and laughed and blushed</b>! I just felt like something was missing,and I think that's because I found Allie's character really <b>flat</b> and indifferent. I couldn't connect with her and even though I didn't hate her, I didn't love her either. This, plus the drug use are the reasons I didn't give it the fifth star! That being said, let's talk about Dean, shall we?<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I do what I want, when I want. And I don’t give a shit what people think about me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The unrepentant manwhore was the most pleasant surprise! There was depth in him I didn't expect to find, and he had a caring side he barely showed that Allie was the one to unlock. I loved the way he interracted with the kids in the team and his discomfort when he was treated differently due to his family and money. Was he vain and cocky? Sure. Was he self-absorbed? Most of the times. But he was also brutally honest about who he was, he never lied nor gave promises he couldn't keep and I must admit I thought he'd run away when things between him and Allie got serious but no, despite his fear he didn't back down and I really admired him for that! And he also oozed sexuality. <b>Compared to Dean Heyward-Di Laurentis, Hell is just a sauna.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454603803ra/17990674.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> did not fail to deliver her trademark humour!</b> The bathtub incident, Allie's ninja moves, the angels talk and the Twilight analysis were some of my favorites, and despite my efforts I couldn't help but burst into maniacal laughter in the middle of the night (because let's face it, it's not a book you can read when your parents are around)! I loved the pop culture references, Dean's relationship with his family and the appearance of the rest of the gang! And holy bananas! the plot twist in the end was a total mindfuck! How on Earth am I supposed to wait for the next book?? There was also enough <b>steam</b> to turn you into a puddle of hormones and <b>holy.hot.chemistry.Batman!</b> Dean and Allie were on fire! And so was I!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454604437ra/17990813.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Being an ordinary girl in an ordinary hockeyless world really sucks.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15940483207943699355" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1269417129" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1269417129" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1269417129?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=sport-hottie">sport-hottie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=oh-my-panties">oh-my-panties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=re-reading">re-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1269417129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4677509244990993455"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>|4.4 stars|<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b> I have the words “I love you” on my lips.<br/>His green eyes burn with emotion. He lets out a husky groan and sags on top of me, thrusting deep one last time. Then he says, “I love you too.”</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Blurb: Allie Hayes is in crisis mode. With graduation looming, she still doesn’t have the first clue about what she's going to do after college. To make matters worse, she’s nursing a broken heart thanks to the end of her longtime relationship. Wild rebound sex is definitely not the solution to her</span>
  <span id="freeText4677509244990993455" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>|4.4 stars|<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> I have the words “I love you” on my lips.<br>His green eyes burn with emotion. He lets out a husky groan and sags on top of me, thrusting deep one last time. Then he says, “I love you too.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Blurb: Allie Hayes is in crisis mode. With graduation looming, she still doesn’t have the first clue about what she's going to do after college. To make matters worse, she’s nursing a broken heart thanks to the end of her longtime relationship. Wild rebound sex is definitely not the solution to her problems, but gorgeous hockey star Dean Di-Laurentis is impossible to resist. Dean always gets what he wants. Girls, grades, girls, recognition, girls…he’s a ladies man, all right, and he’s yet to meet a woman who’s immune to his charms. Until Allie. For one night, the feisty blonde rocked his entire world—and now she wants to be friends? Nope. It’s not over until he says it’s over. Dean is in full-on pursuit, but when life-rocking changes strike, he starts to wonder if maybe it’s time to stop focusing on scoring…and shoot for love.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432989604ra/15033352.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dude, I’m speechless. Elle Kennedy has the magic touch, for real.<br>After me being not really <i>that</i> interested in this third book, she totally rocks my world with the story.<br><br>Once again the characters were absolutely funny, charming and downright adorable and the usual sexiness of the Off-Campus series was on-point. There were a few twists I didn’t see coming, others were rather predictable BUT, boy, did I have fun reading this book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448139252ra/17100130.gif" width="500" height="217" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With The Deal, I fell in love with Garrett and Hannah, in The Mistake I had fun and such adorkable moments with Logan and Grace and with this book? Guys, I had a fucking blast. I laughed so hard I almost fall out of bed, pulled an all-nighter and it was awesome.<br><br>The main couple worked out, despite my early judgement. Their relationship evolved progressively right and flawlessly. If I had any doubt that Dean and Allie couldn’t make it work, Elle just wiped them out.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452562989ra/17708604.gif" width="500" height="189" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alright, so we have Dean. Freaking Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis, you’re made of the stuff wet dreams, smiles and midnight conversations are made of. It was not a secret the guy was smart but I didn’t see coming the whole law school stuff, to be honest. And the fact that he was definitely going for it, it kind of amazed me. I knew the guy was confident but hell that was another level.<br><br>He’s always been the to-go guy if you want so fun and he is/was one of the biggest manwhores I’ve read so far but the thing is, you can’t help but agree in a lot of things with him. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> Stop slut-shaming yourself. And fuck the word slut. People should be able to have sex whenever they want, however many times they want, with however many partners they choose, and not get some shitty label slapped on them.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><u>Have I told you how much I love Elle Kennedy?</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452563069ra/17708611.gif" width="500" height="266" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyways, Dean has many layers and not so many at the same time. He is what he is and he’s not ashamed of it. He loves encouraging people to do what they love and he is against clothing it makes my body ready for the run.<br><br>Dean’s interactions with his family made me want to read about his childhood and how he tried to teach Summer the way of life. I didn’t peg him for a family guy but once you see him teaching those kids? You can’t help but picture him couching his own children. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452562989ra/17708605.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, Allie. *sigh* Girl, you and I came such a long way.<br><br>At first I thought she was cool, you know, in book 1 when we saw her through Hannah and Garrett’s eyes but I couldn’t make much of her other than being a great friend, a fierce girl and stuck in an on-and-off relationship. So, how could I actually like her as a MC right? And that didn’t stop there; I had a tiny hard time loving her for about the first 7-9 chapters. I just couldn’t put the girl Hannah described and this chick who was so afraid of what people may think about her affairs. But what I didn’t realize at the time was that the whole thing was just the result of her relationship with Sean.<br><br>So, once she got over all of that, I could find myself rooting for her and liking her more and more. She’s just such a sweetheart and so wild but at the same time she’s quite down to earth.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446680159ra/16865373.gif" width="500" height="271" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She does little things to honor her mother’s memory that carry incredible weight and that’s pretty cool. She’s really set to make everything work and I just love how funny and open-minded she is.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> “But if you want me to shove Winston up your butt, it’s not happening.”<br>I choke out a laugh. “Don’t worry. I’d prefer it if my butt stayed Winston-free.”<br>“Good.” She lovingly strokes the pink phallus. “Don’t get me wrong—I’ll totally shove whatever you want up there. Just not Winston. He’s special to me.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>This whole scene and what came afterwards had me laughing for about an hour.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450540640ra/17441415.gif" width="500" height="197" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Allie’s relationship with his father is a very healthy one despite her father’s illness. She still wants to do her own things and I rather enjoyed his father’s personality. He was fine.<br><br>What I totally saw coming?<br><br>Dean’s career change. From the moment coach O’Shera said he was to train those kids? Yep, I knew it right there.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452562989ra/17708606.gif" width="350" height="197" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I totally <b>did not</b> see coming?<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Beau’s death. Seriously, I thought Allie’s father was going to die so that took me by surprise. I won’t lie and say I cried but I did feel so so sad. Beau was a great guy and an actually constant figure in the books. It was very unexpected. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413619306ra/11537922.gif" width="476" height="253" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Allie and Dean as a couple is the cutest thing ever. Why? Because they’re so fucking sexy and they laugh so much. They make each other really happy. I think they discover a little more about themselves each day but more importantly? They support each other in any way they can. They won’t cut their wings for the other person and that’s just the way it’s supposed to be.<br><br>Like, they're so<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452562989ra/17708607.gif" width="500" height="263" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but they're also so<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398819766ra/9468385.gif" width="500" height="242" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, overall and against the odds, this book was such a pleasant surprise. I honestly wasn’t expecting to be this involved in their relationship but having them making me laugh and sigh so hard, well, it was bound to happen. Now, my two questions are:<br><br>1). Is Dean’s sister going to be a future MC? Are we going to see her and Fitz in the future? She could totally transfer…<br><br>2). <u>What the fuck with Tuck?</u> <br>That was so out of the blue and with <i>her?</i> The next book is going to be pretty interesting to read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452562989i/17708608.gif" width="485" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4677509244990993455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1442089805" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1442089805" />
    <a title="Sleepless Readmore" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29809756-sleepless-readmore"><img alt="Sleepless Readmore" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608469p2/29809756.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1442089805?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sleepless Readmore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sleepless Readmore" href="/user/show/29809756-sleepless-readmore">Sleepless Readmore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29809756-sleepless-readmore?shelf=5-star-books">5-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29809756-sleepless-readmore?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1442089805" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5228357538765121576"><b>She is art.</b> What the f*ck do you <b>expect</b> from her,<br/>Other than confusion, <b>beauty</b>, and goddamn soul?<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429609332i/14611766.png' width='407' height='173' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>5</b> #HeWants<b>HerOnA</b>BiologicalLevel <b>STARS</b><br/><br/><i>Allie</i> <b>and</b> <i>Dean</i> .. ♥<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452599188i/17713728._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Dean</b>. Oh sweetheart I've <b>been waiting</b> for your book. I certainly <b>WAS NOT</b> disappointed with this one. The <i>biggest player</i> out of the hockey bunch who I've fallen <b>head over heels</b> for. One thing that was <u>constant</u> was my smile. Whether it be <b>a watery one</b> or one from laughter. <i>Dean</i> never failed to keep one on my face. This guy is <b>HILARIOUS</b>, sweet, and </span>
  <span id="freeText5228357538765121576" style="display:none"><b>She is art.</b> What the f*ck do you <b>expect</b> from her,<br>Other than confusion, <b>beauty</b>, and goddamn soul?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429609332i/14611766.png" width="407" height="173" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>5</b> #HeWants<b>HerOnA</b>BiologicalLevel <b>STARS</b><br><br><i>Allie</i> <b>and</b> <i>Dean</i> .. ♥<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452599188i/17713728._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dean</b>. Oh sweetheart I've <b>been waiting</b> for your book. I certainly <b>WAS NOT</b> disappointed with this one. The <i>biggest player</i> out of the hockey bunch who I've fallen <b>head over heels</b> for. One thing that was <u>constant</u> was my smile. Whether it be <b>a watery one</b> or one from laughter. <i>Dean</i> never failed to keep one on my face. This guy is <b>HILARIOUS</b>, sweet, and <u>quite</u> the looker. <i>Allie</i> scored with this one although <i>Allie</i> is pretty amazing herself. I adored <b>the banter</b> between these two and their story was <u>EPIC</u> per usual (wouldn't expect anything less from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a>). I've learned to <b>expect the unexpected</b> with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> novels which I love because the plot isn't <u>always</u> predictable.<br><br><blockquote>"Ugh. You even have perfect nipples," <b>I gripe</b>.<br><b>His lips twitch.</b> "Do you wanna touch em?"</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455314902ra/18087145.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>"I am perfect. I need to remind myself of that more often."<br><b>I snort.</b> "Right. Because you're not conceited enough."<br>"I'm confident," <b>he corrects.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>The Boys.</b> I've said it once and I'll say it again .. <u>I LOVE THESE BROTHERS</u>. I love how they live together, how they are <b>ALWAYS</b> there for one another, and how they talk to one another! Honestly where does <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> come up with this <i>BRILLIANT</i> dialogue?! It is <u>GOLDEN</u>. I use to think that football players were my favourite but of course after reading about <b>hockey players</b> .. I switched over! Normally when I read the <i>next book in a series</i> I'll end up loving those characters <b>more than the first</b> and then cycle continues. With these novels .. I enjoyed <i>all the characters</i> and wouldn't be able to pick <b>ONE</b> favourite couple.<br><br><blockquote>"Edward wants her on a biological level, right?"<br>"Are you seriously dissecting Twilight right now?"<br><b>God, I am. This is what Allie has reduced me to.<br>A sad, pathetic loser who goes to a bar and forces<br>his friend to to participate in a Twilight book club.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455314902ra/18087146.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>He looks at the bathtub, <br>where I'm lounging like Cleo-fuck-ing-patra.<br>He looks at the bubbles surrounding my body <br>like a fluffy white clod. And then he looks at Winston.<br><b>"Dude,"</b> I blurt out. <b>"It's not what it looks like!"</b><br><b>"Nope, nope, nope, I don't want to know!"</b><br>Snatches his pants off the rack. Continues backing away. <br>His eyes again focus on the pink dildo two inches from my hand.<br>I try again. <b>"I promise you, it's not --"</b><br><b>"I don't want to know."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455314902ra/18087147.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>"I was a perfect gentlemen."<br><b>Logan snorts.</b> "Well, that's a first."<br>"Fuck you very much. I happen to be skilled in the art of gentlemanry."<br>"That's not an art. Or a work." <b>Logan rolls his eyes.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>The Series.</b> This is my <b>go to</b>, my all star, my most <b>recommended</b> NA one. I do <u>NOT</u> want it to end and it <i>breaks my heart</i> knowing there is only <u>ONE</u> more left. Although, I will be continuously <b>re-reading</b> it. I saw a lot of <u>potential</u> in this author and the series keeps getting <b>BETTER</b> and <u>BETTER</u> (if that's even possible). I love the way the <i>stories intertwine</i> and I get to continuously read about familiar faces. Each novel has it's own <b>unique love story</b> and I <u>HIGHLY</u> recommend reading them if you <s>haven't so</s> already.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Every little thing she does is magic<br>Every thing she does just turns me on ..<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9ifR2A9Afbk" rel="nofollow noopener">►♫</a></i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455314902ra/18087148.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>"You're lucky I love you, babe. <br>If any other girl had done this to me --"<br><b>"You love me? You just said it."</b><br>"I ... Well, damn. I guess I did."<br><b>"Did you mean it? I want to hear it again."</b><br>"Aw shit, babe. Don't make me say it again.<br>It's bad enough I said it first."</blockquote><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27252717.The_Score__Off_Campus___3_" title="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Score</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429608985i/14611753.png" width="335" height="204" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1431282052s/24920901.jpg" alt="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564665.The_Mistake__Off_Campus___2_" title="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1447598937s/25564665.jpg" alt="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27252717.The_Score__Off_Campus___3_" title="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1447303226s/27252717.jpg" alt="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1439821135" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1439821135" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1439821135?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=standalone-in-series">standalone-in-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1439821135" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer232751554777386937"><b>
  <u>FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED:</u>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You’re going about this the wrong way, you know. The best way to get over someone is to hook up with someone else. ASAP.”<br/>“I’m not ready to be with anyone else yet.”<br/>“Sure you are. Seriously, just find yourself a rebound.” Dean whips up his arm. “I volunteer as tribute.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Just when I thought this series could not get any better, we are given another delectable instalment in this witty, sexy, flawlessly written series about opposites attracting. We saw the cock</span>
  <span id="freeText232751554777386937" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED:</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You’re going about this the wrong way, you know. The best way to get over someone is to hook up with someone else. ASAP.”<br>“I’m not ready to be with anyone else yet.”<br>“Sure you are. Seriously, just find yourself a rebound.” Dean whips up his arm. “I volunteer as tribute.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Just when I thought this series could not get any better, we are given another delectable instalment in this witty, sexy, flawlessly written series about opposites attracting. We saw the cocky team captain fall for a sassy geek in <a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2015/02/16/the-deal-elle-kennedy/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Deal</a>, the star defenseman fight for a second chance in <a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2015/04/24/the-mistake-by-elle-kennedy/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mistake</a>, and now we get to properly meet another star of the Briar hockey team—the team’s resident party animal and the biggest player on the planet—and the spirited blonde who ends up rocking his world. These stories are such guilty pleasures of mine, a fun and utterly addictive reading experience beginning to end, and Dean and Allie’s story did not disappoint in the slightest.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“So I’m…what, your relationship sponsor? I’m the one who makes sure you don’t fall off the wagon?”<br>“Yep. Congratulations, you finally get to do something worthwhile with your time,” I say sarcastically.<br>He tips his head. “What do I get in return?”<br>“The satisfaction of knowing you’re helping someone other than yourself?”<br>“Naah. How about a BJ? I’ll do it for a BJ.”<br>I give him the finger. “You wish.”<br>“Fine, an HJ.”</i>
</blockquote><br>An incorrigible ladies’ man who always gets whatever he wants, whenever he wants it, Dean Hayward-Di Laurentis’ lighthearted attitude gives the impression that he doesn’t have a worry in the world, but behind the team’s star defenseman’s confident swagger lies a man who has not found his true direction in life. Born to privilege and expected to follow in his parents’ footsteps, Dean passes his college days focusing on hockey, random hook-ups, and spending time with his friends, his innate intelligence hidden behind a careless, live-in-the-moment stance on life. But when an unexpected one-night stand turns into the greatest sexual experience of his life, Dean finds himself in uncharted territory, unable to stop thinking about the first woman in his life who’s left him craving for more.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The memories come crashing back in vivid Technicolor. The terrible movie. The tequila shots. The…rest. I slept with Dean last night. Twice. My heart beats faster as I stare up at the ceiling. I’m in Dean’s room. There’s an empty condom wrapper on the end table. And…yep, I’m naked. Maybe it was a bad dream, a voice in my head tries to assure me. I draw another deep breath and find the courage to turn my head. What I encounter seizes my lungs again. A very naked Dean is stretched out on his stomach. His bare ass taunts me, not just with its sheer perfection, but because of the red scratches on his tight butt cheeks. My nails had left those scratches. I lift a weak hand and notice the fingernail on my index finger is broken. I broke a nail while clawing at Dean’s ass.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Allie Hayes cannot believe she let the biggest flirt on the planet seduce her, but a night of wild, drunken monkey sex is exactly what her heart needed to get over a painful breakup. She might feel disgusted with herself the morning after, and determined to never let it happen again, but Allie is not a woman who lingers on regrets, and moving on is exactly what she plans on doing from the moment she flees the ‘scene of the crime’. Unfortunately, the man in question does not happen to be on the same page.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Hey. What’s up?”<br>I let out a ragged breath. “I want to f*ck you again.”<br>“Is this a thing now? You’re going to call me every night and say that?”<br>“Maybe?” Shit. I’m cranky and horny and as confused as she is. “Say yes, baby doll. Just say yes and put me out of my misery.”</i>
</blockquote><br>So a tantalising game of cat-and-mouse begins between two people who have very little in common at first, but the more they get to know about one another, the more they realise that appearances can be deceiving. Allie’s feisty personality and blind ambition are no match for her selfless heart, and she soon discovers that Dean’s confident, well-adjusted façade hides a vulnerable young man whose unconditional love can also become his greatest downfall.<br><br>As always, this story was the perfect blend of heart-warming romance and amusing, engaging dialogues, woven through a well-balanced plotline that entertains and touches our hearts in equal measure. I loved these characters, I loved how multi-layered they got as their story unfolded, and I never wanted to part with them. The premise of a notorious womanizer falling for the first woman to resist his charms might appear cliché at first, but there is nothing cliché about this story, there is nothing cliché about the way these characters are brought to life, and there is nothing cliché about this author’s extraordinary ability to deliver a story that always feels fresh, unique, and exciting. A great addition to the series and a top recommendation from me.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“A blond Adonis with his golden chest and sculpted muscles and perfectly chiseled face. If the hockey thing doesn’t work out for him, he ought to consider going into modeling. Dean Di Laurentis oozes sexuality. He could slap his face on a laxative label and every woman in the world would be praying for constipation just to have an excuse to buy it.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://natbkj.me/the-score" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a><br><br><strong><a href="http://amzn.to/20Lx1zf" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> | <a href="http://amzn.to/1NJcZ3l" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a> | <a href="http://amzn.to/1HGLW1Z" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon CA</a> | <a href="https://geo.itunes.apple.com/us/book/the-score/id1050857569?mt=11&amp;at=1l3vttd" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">iBooks</a> | <a href="http://amzn.to/1Scs9R2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Paperback</a></strong></span>

</a><br/><br/><br/>To say I was a little excited to read <b>The Score</b> is a bit of an understatement...<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20II/5665DDBA-A466-4702-B3FE-19B26B7A1E7E_zpsio8zvjqc.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450817534ra/17472153.gif' alt=' photo 5665DDBA-A466-4702-B3FE-19B26B7A1E7E_zpsio8zvjqc.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>I mean, this is <b>Elle Kennedy, </b>who has proven to me she is the queen of arrogant yet completely endearing man-whores (and she's actually making me enjoy the NA genre again- which is a huge undertaking in itself). I'd met <b>Dean Di Laurentis </b>in<i> The Deal </i>and knew this self-absorbed sex-on-a-stick would give us an entertaining ride. To say this book is</span>
  <span id="freeText11208322952322595324" style="display:none"><i>It's live! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1R5Pq7q">http://amzn.to/1R5Pq7q</a></i><br><br><b>5+ "I don't like shirts" Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/review%20art/EA858A34-7B36-45DE-8408-FBCB4A8A89F5_zpspkrufijx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450817534i/17472152._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo EA858A34-7B36-45DE-8408-FBCB4A8A89F5_zpspkrufijx.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>To say I was a little excited to read <b>The Score</b> is a bit of an understatement...<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20II/5665DDBA-A466-4702-B3FE-19B26B7A1E7E_zpsio8zvjqc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450817534ra/17472153.gif" alt=" photo 5665DDBA-A466-4702-B3FE-19B26B7A1E7E_zpsio8zvjqc.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I mean, this is <b>Elle Kennedy, </b>who has proven to me she is the queen of arrogant yet completely endearing man-whores (and she's actually making me enjoy the NA genre again- which is a huge undertaking in itself). I'd met <b>Dean Di Laurentis </b>in<i> The Deal </i>and knew this self-absorbed sex-on-a-stick would give us an entertaining ride. To say this book is entertaining is such a gross understatement. The sheer number of highlights is proof positive that <b>The Score</b> will rival the likes of Garrett and Hannah's <i>The Deal. </i>Each book in this series can be read as a stand-alone but I'd still read them all as they're that good- and all revolve around a team of sexy hockey players at Briar College. So without further ado....<br><br>I introduce the man of the hour- the man who hates shirts, lives for sex, hockey, and his own uber inflated ego- <b>Dean Di Laurentis...</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20II/3DED57AD-1F3C-476E-B2EF-8B115B432DD4_zpszk5bhfih.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450817534ra/17472154.gif" alt=" photo 3DED57AD-1F3C-476E-B2EF-8B115B432DD4_zpszk5bhfih.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>Here's a tissue...you're drooling on yourself...</i><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Dean Di Laurentis oozes sexuality. He could slap his face on a laxative label and every woman in the world would be praying for constipation just to have an excuse to buy it.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>When Hannah's roommate <b>Allie Hayes</b> has a messy break-up with her 3-year boyfriend, she's looking for a place to hide. She's avoiding Sean as she knows her will is weak and she really wants a clean break. So Garrett offers up his room at their house for the weekend. He and Hannah will be out of town so his room is empty. Just Tucker and Dean will be around. With a few errant texts to Dean to <i>keep it in his pants</i>, the plan is set. <br><blockquote>
  <b><br>Garrett:</b>
  <i> Allie’s gonna crash in my room.</i>
  <b><br>Garrett:</b>
  <i> Your dick can stay in your room.</i>
</blockquote><br>When Allie shows at the house, it's apparent Dean did not receive the texts and interrupting his current threesome doesn't go over well. Dean instead finds himself<s> cockblocked with blue balls</s> babysitting a broken hearted and off-limits 'Hannah BFF,' Allie. <i>Fun times. </i> So they tap open a bottle of tequila, and you know what they say about tequila and clothes....a trip to the <i>bone zone.</i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20II/3AE561A3-89B8-4E8C-A38F-20DDBD086982_zpscerssib0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450817535ra/17472155.gif" alt=" photo 3AE561A3-89B8-4E8C-A38F-20DDBD086982_zpscerssib0.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Allie</b> doesn't do casual sex yet she finds herself waking to a very naked Dean beside her and visions of a crazy night full of everything sexual fantasies are made of. No wonder Dean has the reputation of screwing half the female student body at Briar. But it's a one and done. She doesn't do hook-ups and definitely not with the notorious <b>Dean Di Laurentis.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To say I enjoyed <b>Dean</b> and <b>Allie's </b>story is a massive understatement. Dean is beyond endearing in all his humorous yet arrogant ways and combine his sexual prowess, Allie doesn't stand a chance. I loved everything about each one of them. First, Allie is real. She has her convictions and she tries damn hard to stay true to them. Second, she's confident in her sexuality. Holy mother of<i> lip-biting-till-he-bleeds </i>scenes. Their chemistry is off the charts SMOKING and I commend the author for giving us a heroine that is confident in taking what she wants from a delicious piece of manmeat!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20II/AA0F24A6-8AE6-497F-9D76-287C26A04C10_zps9tvmtgtf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450817535ra/17472156.gif" alt=" photo AA0F24A6-8AE6-497F-9D76-287C26A04C10_zps9tvmtgtf.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>But, for once, <b>Allie </b>wants this to be a one-time hook-up and nothing more yet<b> Dean</b> is not satisfied with just once. Sex with Allie was beyond anything he'd ever experienced. He finally finds <i>that girl</i> and she says "one and done?" Say it isn't so! Allie won't do casual. She wants strings so that doesn't include <b>the</b> Dean Di Laurentis, Briar College man-whore extraordinaire.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><br>The only problem is—I like the strings. Sex and relationships go hand in hand for me. I’m all about the snuggling and inside jokes and talking late into the night. I’m a card-carrying member of Team Boyfriend, and after last night, I can honestly say that Team One-Night-Stand sucks balls. The sex was incredible, but the shame it left me with isn’t worth the orgasms.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>But Dean tends to disagree. What Dean, wants Dean gets...<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/review%20art/5D09FC67-747F-4723-8694-8C1592F464D1_zpso0tkxnf5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451139136i/17510898._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5D09FC67-747F-4723-8694-8C1592F464D1_zpso0tkxnf5.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I loved the progression of their love story. Not an insta-love but more of a combustion that trickles to a slow build again. The growth of both these characters together was phenomenal and secondary characters just added to their draw. Dean is a guy not many people have a lot of faith in beyond sex and having a good time but he really surprises us all here...and Allie is his kryptonite, his deal breaker. <i>Little Dean</i> only has eyes for Allie.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I mean you’re facing a Jacob quandary. You imprinted on her pussy, and now it’s the only pussy you can think about. You exist solely for this pussy. Like Jacob and that weird mutant baby.” <br><br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>There is NOTHING I would change about this book. We have humor, steam, a bit of (mature) drama, just <b>everything. <i>The Score </i></b> is a fantastic third installment in the Off-Campus series. Looking forward to more from Elle Kennedy!<br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Advanced copy received by author in exchange for my honest review. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/scroll%20Art/4AB7D2EF-98B8-46FC-A9C6-7DBA4C8C2037_zpsodd2uyue.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449143214i/17241440.jpg" alt=" photo 4AB7D2EF-98B8-46FC-A9C6-7DBA4C8C2037_zpsodd2uyue.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/allipalk" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <br><br></i></span>

And <b>HOT</b>. One of the hockey hotties of Briar, this guy is the manwhore of all manwhores in the team. And</span>

And <b>HOT</b>. Who wouldn't get all warmed-up when it's <i>The Life of Dean</i> we're talking here? <b>DEAN SEBASTIAN KENDRICK HEYWARD-DI LAURENTIS</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428260344ra/14397035.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We've met <b>Dean</b> in the previous books of the <b>Off-Campus</b> series. One of the hockey hotties of Briar, this guy is the manwhore of all manwhores in the team. And then there's <b>Allie Hayes</b>, Hannah's (Garrett's girlfriend) best friend who also appeared in the previous books, who just broke-up with her long-term boyfriend Sean. Things started off when Allie went to the hockey players' apartment to spend the night in order to avoid being confronted by Sean. That's the time when she and Dean got drunk together and well, ended up screwing each other.<br><br>This book is practically a <i>friends-with-benefits</i> kind of book, but I loved how the romance came out very developed here-- how Dean and Allie both started off as f*ck buddies which turned into something in the long run. And of course, their character development. So amazed how Dean transformed into one responsible and matured guy and how he stayed loyal to only one girl. *sigh<br><br>As usual, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> once again made this entire book worth the read because of the humor that's present in every chapter. There were LOTS of laughable moments here. <b>Little Dean, WINSTON, the martial arts done by Allie and Summer, the Hunger Games and Twilight references, Logan and G's teasings, Tuck's shenanigans, and all!</b>. I had to take a break just to have a good, healthy laugh!!! And my, those hot scenes-- NUFF SAID.<br><br>Seriously, this installment is everything. Dean is one of the NA men every girl would really swoon over. I enjoyed everything here because it's so damn entertaining and romantic to the extreme! I need the fourth book now!<br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993136i/16730745.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>

<span id="freeTextContainer5059010144697302073">Update it's now LIVE!!!<br/><br/><b> 5 stars! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/score%20collage.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451015912i/17499296.png' alt=' photo score collage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>You know the book is a winner when you have a smile on your face the entire time you’re reading it. Considering I have loved every Elle Kennedy book I’ve read, I knew going into this book it would be a good read. What I didn’t know is that I would freaking love this book. I need to get my hands on a paperback copy so I can hug it very tightly! <br/><br/><b> The Score </b> begins with Allie having just broken up with her boyfriend. Knowing how easily he can worm his way back i</span>
  <span id="freeText5059010144697302073" style="display:none">Update it's now LIVE!!!<br><br><b> 5 stars! </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/score%20collage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451015912i/17499296.png" alt=" photo score collage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You know the book is a winner when you have a smile on your face the entire time you’re reading it. Considering I have loved every Elle Kennedy book I’ve read, I knew going into this book it would be a good read. What I didn’t know is that I would freaking love this book. I need to get my hands on a paperback copy so I can hug it very tightly! <br><br><b> The Score </b> begins with Allie having just broken up with her boyfriend. Knowing how easily he can worm his way back into her life, she asks her friends for sanctuary and her friend’s boyfriend Garrett offers Allie his place for the weekend while they’re gone. Allie runs over to his place to find his roommate Dean there, the campus manwhore. The two hang out for the night and something happens between them. But in the light of day Allie doesn’t want to continue and Dean wants more.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451015912ra/17499297.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well I don’t want to get all spoilery and tell the entire plot, so I will do my best to keep this review spoiler free like the author requested. I will say I literally laughed out loud while reading this book, many many times. Especially a certain bathtub scene that some of you have come to know and love. The banter between Dean and Allie was my favorite part about this whole book, they kept each other on their toes. <br><br>I also loved how for Dean and Allie they didn’t expect anything from the other, and in return they both ended up needing each other for different reasons. Dean may have had a playboy exterior, but beneath that façade he was so much more, and Allie was the one to see past it and accept Dean for the wonderful man he was. Dean and Allie are one of my favorite book couples, I think they are perfect together. <br><br>I gotta say, Elle Kennedy continues to impress and she is an author who I will forever read and recommend. If you haven’t read anything by her yet, get on it!!<br><br><i> ARC kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review </i> <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/RRR.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

A perfect escape from boring reality – something I desperately needed this year. <br/><br/>The Deal and The Mistake – wh</span>
  <span id="freeText7631862344024494400" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> The Score<br><b>Series:</b> Off Campus #3<br><b>Author:</b> Elle Kennedy<br><b>Release Date: </b> 16 January, 2016<br><b>Rating:</b> 4 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How much I enjoy reading Elle Kennedy ’s Off – Campus Series is indescribable. Gah! The sizzling chemistry and intense intimacy between the MCs is what makes those books so freaking awesome! They are just so damn good and funny! A perfect escape from boring reality – something I desperately needed this year. <br><br>The Deal and The Mistake – which I’ve read few months before, were so good they both made it to my list of top picks of 2015. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451472417i/17547345.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“I’m not ready to be with anyone else yet.”<br>“Sure you are. Seriously, just find yourself a rebound.” Dean whips up his arm. “I volunteer as tribute.”</b><br><br>The Score, newest addition to Kennedy’s series, is not disappointing either. It delivered exactly what I’ve been craving from NA and had everything I learned to expect from Kennedy’s work: great banter, hot sex scenes, swoony and touching moments and fabulous characters! It was flirty, sexy and damn cute. We have tons of lust, lots of sassiness and wittiness, a tad bit of drama and complex, vivid characters you won’t be able to not fall in love with. See, I am still all gooey inside.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434069758i/15173130._SX540_.png" width="400" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I decided to not give away any plot details here – if you really want some info just check all those awesome reviews of my friends; the best though, is to meet the characters by yourself and slowly unravel all of the elements of the novel. Especially because it is very similar in trend to the previous books. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451472542i/17547366.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Dean Di Laurentis oozes sexuality. He could slap his face on a laxative label and every woman in the world would be praying for constipation just to have an excuse to buy it."</b><br><br><br>My only concern and something that put me off a little bit is the repetitiveness of the story – it really is a copy of previous books – same things happen, the characters are very similar in behavior, their relationships are alike and.. to be frank there was nothing fresh or different about it. Same story told in the same way – with great humor (trademark of Kennedy’s), fantastic style of writing and scorching sex. And while I did have a lot of fun (how could I not?) I was still worried about it. And I certainly hope that in the future releases Elle Kennedy will do everything in her power to take her work into another level so the storyline will be refreshed and more surprising. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434069758i/15173130._SX540_.png" width="400" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On the other hand, I am sure that every fan of Off – Campus boys will be thrilled and super excited while reading Dean and Allie’s story. I believe that high expectations of almost everyone will be met. It’s good, satisfying and dirty story so be sure to check it out!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451472542i/17547367.jpg" width="400" height="220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434069758i/15173130._SX540_.png" width="400" height="90" <span id="freeTextContainer11234500351870853349"><i> FULL REVIEW POSTED! </i><br/><b> <i> 4.99 "Dean+Allie+Winston"stars </i></b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Allie am I interrupting you while you're,um...riding the solo train to Orgasmville?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452520815ra/17702996.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>When Elle Kennedy <i>strikes</i>, she <b>scores</b>!!!<br/><br/><b>With this book she out done herself! Once again showed that she's brilliant author with <u>unique style!</u></b><br/><br/>Despite that the words <b><u>float</u> to me like <i>drinking mohitto in a hot summer day</i></b>, I felt this book! <u>I laughed, I cried, I was angry, I swoooned, I was happy, I felt everything and i couldn't put it down for a de</u></span>
  <span id="freeText11234500351870853349" style="display:none"><i> FULL REVIEW POSTED! </i><br><b> <i> 4.99 "Dean+Allie+Winston"stars </i></b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Allie am I interrupting you while you're,um...riding the solo train to Orgasmville?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452520815ra/17702996.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When Elle Kennedy <i>strikes</i>, she <b>scores</b>!!!<br><br><b>With this book she out done herself! Once again showed that she's brilliant author with <u>unique style!</u></b><br><br>Despite that the words <b><u>float</u> to me like <i>drinking mohitto in a hot summer day</i></b>, I felt this book! <u>I laughed, I cried, I was angry, I swoooned, I was happy, I felt everything and i couldn't put it down for a dear life !!!</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393489697ra/8721390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What i loved about the story.. well besides <b>EVERYTHING</b>, I seriously love the humour, the love, the banters, the storyline, the progress of their relationship and the friendships. It was highly entertaining to read about Twilight and what was most amusing was that the conversation about it was leading by the boys. Nothing hotter than men reading or watching the movies, we the girls love! <i>*sigh*</i> Plus the conversation was <b> HILARIOUS </b>!<br><br><b>“You know, I don’t think we’re dealing with a Bella’s-magical-blood situation here.”<br>“No?”<br>“No. I think you’ve imprinted on this girl’s pussy.”<br>… “What do you mean?”<br>“I mean you’re facing a Jacob quandary. You imprinted on her pussy, and now it’s the only pussy you can think about. You exist solely for this pussy. Like Jacob and that weird mutant baby.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440448311ra/15976482.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Allie</b> just got herself out of a toxic relationship and all she wanted was to feel free from men but then she was at <i>Dean's house.</i> They were alone, they got alcohol and one thing led to another. Two people who never got a one normal conversation found their perfect language in bed! She tried to avoid him afterwards, to pretend like nothing had happened but they both knew that it was impossible to forget. The passion, the heat, the chemistry was <b>OFF CHARTS</b> and the one night stand turns out to be something <i>impossible to leave without.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453545287ra/17839536.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Dean Di Laurentis is in my blood now. I didn’t expect the intense sexual chemistry between us, but it’s here, and it’s addictive, and I don’t know how I can ever give it up.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453545671ra/17839617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Allie was an <b>amazing heroine!</b> So strong, been through so much and still dealing with so much but she manages to live her life and fight for her dreams. She was funny as hell! She wasn't afraid to speak her mind, to say what she wants and her inner monologues made me laugh so hard. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He looks at the bathtub, where I’m lounging like Cleo-fucking-patra.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><u>This girl was fierce, along with Wellsy! Their friendship was beautiful!</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451781390ra/17604409.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dean.. I want to be his babydoll, his <u>VIVI</u>cat and everything!</b> He was the rich boy who lives his life how he wants, do whatever he wants and wherever he wants. Despite what labels everyone put on him he wasn't what everyone thought. <u>He was smart, caring, funny (every character in this series is funny!!!) and sooo sweet!</u> He was hot for Allie 24/7 but it wasn't all about the sex. He and Allie were so much alike. They wanted to be carefree and enjoy their moments together. Although the sex.. oh boy! This was by far the sexiest book in the series!!<br><b>Made me hot a looooot!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <b>
    <i>"It's me. You want me. And as long as this hungry pu*&amp;y keeps dripping for me, we're not fu&amp;*ing done."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453545287ra/17839537.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I love her shamelessness, how she's up for anything and completely unapologetic about it. Just like me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453545287ra/17839538.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>It was brilliant!</b> This book was everything I could ask for. Sport romance, full with funny, steamy, alluring and amazing writing style! I didn't want to put my Kindle down, I didn't want to sleep so yep, I stayed till the late hours in my bed and read!<br><br><b>“I’m adorable, first off. My sense of humor is stellar—obvs.”<br>“Obvs,” she echoes dryly.<br>“I’m extraordinarily skilled in the art of conversation.”<br>She nods. “When it’s about yourself, of course.”<br>“Of course.” I pretend to think it over some more. “Oh, and I’m a mind reader. No lie. I always know what the other person is thinking.”<br>“Yeah? What am I thinking right now?” Allie challenges.<br>“That you want me to shut up and fuck you again.”<br>She shakes her head in dismay. “Goddamn it. That’s actually what I was thinking.”<br>I smirk at her and tap my forehead. “Told ya. Mind reader.” </b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Garrett: Allie's gonna crash in my room.<br>Garrett: Your dick can stay in your room.” </i>
</b><br><br><b> Basically I was like that... </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451058197ra/17503184.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh and the bathtub scene!!! Winston was a real member of this story, folks! LOL<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453545287ra/17839539.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The <u>bromance</u> in this book was strong and amazing and that's why I was so<b> heartbroken</b> when the things went wrong but I guess that's real life and indeed things like these happens and people got hurt but still, it was really sad and unfortunate!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447128610ra/16961325.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why not 5 full stars? </b><br>Well because I don't appreciate using <i>any kind</i> of drugs. Drugs are something I am strongly against and reading about them is bugging me in some ways. But in the end I forgot about that I was too consumed to the story !!! The minute I finished the book I want to re-read it so do yourself a favor and <b> READ THIS BOOK!!! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443123091ra/16320645.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1267934678" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1267934678" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267934678?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=advanced-copy">advanced-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=auto-buy-author">auto-buy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=athlete-mc">athlete-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=top-shelf-quality">top-shelf-quality</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=new-adult-college">new-adult-college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=mr-money-bags">mr-money-bags</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267934678" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7702080240469068659"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> The Score<br/><b>Series:</b> Off-Campus #3<br/><b>Author:</b> Elle Kennedy<br/><b>Release date: </b> January 11, 2016<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b>HEA</b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450725233i/17460411.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series for me has been nothing short of magic. And I don't throw out those words lightly. I've gone through so many NA books that were passable, but just didn't have anything special to differentiate them from any of the others in the genre. What makes this series so great is that every single book has been memorable enough to land them on my favorites </span>
  <span id="freeText7702080240469068659" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> The Score<br><b>Series:</b> Off-Campus #3<br><b>Author:</b> Elle Kennedy<br><b>Release date: </b> January 11, 2016<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b>HEA</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450725233i/17460411.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series for me has been nothing short of magic. And I don't throw out those words lightly. I've gone through so many NA books that were passable, but just didn't have anything special to differentiate them from any of the others in the genre. What makes this series so great is that every single book has been memorable enough to land them on my favorites shelf. They're packed with flawless banter, and a genuine quality you find in not only the romance, but the friendships between the entire group of characters. The wittiness between Garrett, Logan, Dean and Tucker has been a bromance made in heaven. They love to bust each other's balls on a daily basis and that makes me one happy reader to be able to get a front seat for the show. I've become so attached to this group, it almost feels like coming home when I get to revisit them again with in every new story.<br><br>I've been waiting with bated breath for Dean's book. The college manwhore athlete is not a new concept, yet I had every faith that Elle Kennedy would infuse life right back into it and put her own original stamp on it. And let me set your fears aside right now, she once again has delivered a well executed story. The manwhore hero is not always a winning character for me, but Dean completely won me over-with one cocky wink and glimpse of his shameless swagger, I was charmed. He's just so <i>completely over-the-top</i> sinfully sexy and confident, you can't help but fall for his shamefulness. But the cherry on top of the manwhore cupcake was his complete and utter reform, and his surprisingly emotional path to becoming a better man.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450725233i/17460412.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dean has always been portrayed as sex obsessed and simply put: only out for physical pleasure. His own, and any girl who's willing to partake with him. He's the jokester, the one who doesn't take life too seriously. People tend to underestimate him. But we get to see a whole other side to him in The Score, and though he had his faults, he also had some hidden facets that will be sure to surprise you. His sweetness was just adorable as he was discovering his feelings for Allie were rooting deeper than he had anticipated. And yeah, he had that dirty side to him just as you'd expect and It. Was. Good.<br><br><b>"Get over yourself," I mutter. "I'd be wet if any guy was rubbing up against me."<br>"Bull. Fucking. Shit." His thumb brushes my clit. I almost fall over. <br>"It's me. You want <i>me.</i></b><br><br>Allie was a fantastic heroine. She turned out to be perfectly paired with Dean in several ways. She was adventurous, and blunt. She was bold and strong, and refused to accept being Dean's temporary plaything. I loved seeing her put him in his place and cut his confidence down a size or two.<br><br><b>"My face? Turn-on. Chest? Turn-on. I'd roll over and show you my ass, but we both know the answer will be 'turn-on' so I'll skip that one. Dick? Turn the fuck on. And then we get to the non-physical awesomeness that is Dean."<br>"Speaking in the third person? Not a turn-on."</b><br><br>She demanded respect and she gave it back in return when he let her in and showed her the side of himself that no one else gets to see. It all started with an embarrassing one night stand, and Allie vows to move on and forget it ever happened. She's still in recovery mode from her recent break up with her long time boyfriend. While Dean was a good time, he's not boyfriend material. And she's not a casual sex type of girl. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450725233i/17460413.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unfortunately for her, Dean develops a surprising obsession for her since that night and they're both drifting in uncharted territory. The man who is used to getting everything he's ever wanted suddenly has a hunger that can't be quenched. And Allie? She's just trying to mend her broken heart, not break it all over again. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450725234i/17460414.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They lead each other on a merry chase that will leave you spellbound. I just can't express the hilarity, the explosive chemistry, and the poignant levels that this book attains. My smiles were too many to count. They both had hurdles to overcome, growing to do, and path to get there was not an easy one. None of the drama felt overdone or unnecessary however. Everything had a purpose and was explored with sensitivity. This book is the total package, I couldn't give it less than five enthusiastic stars. Obviously I highly recommend this one, but don't take my word for it. Go march your fingers to that Amazon one-click button on release day and judge for yourself. The entertainment value you'll find in this one is priceless. <br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow
