<span id="freeTextContainer13969033026787771741"><b>5 "Little Dean" STARS</b><br/><br/>This series is just the bomb! Elle delivers another great addition about these hockey hotties from Briar University. This was definitely a score!<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/dcTBKyz' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450627578ra/17449848.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The third book in this series is about Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis, the sexy, rich, D-man of the Briar's hockey team and the unabashed manwhore. And Hannah's BFF and roommate, Allie Hayes, the sexy, sassy and smart drama major and life long nester - she only does relationships. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/the%20score_zpsqhlsy2t4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450627342i/17449833._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo the score_zpsqhlsy2t4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>These two are brought together</span>
  <span id="freeText13969033026787771741" style="display:none"><b>5 "Little Dean" STARS</b><br><br>This series is just the bomb! Elle delivers another great addition about these hockey hotties from Briar University. This was definitely a score!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/dcTBKyz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450627578ra/17449848.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The third book in this series is about Dean Sebastian Kendrick Heyward-Di Laurentis, the sexy, rich, D-man of the Briar's hockey team and the unabashed manwhore. And Hannah's BFF and roommate, Allie Hayes, the sexy, sassy and smart drama major and life long nester - she only does relationships. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/the%20score_zpsqhlsy2t4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450627342i/17449833._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo the score_zpsqhlsy2t4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>These two are brought together as Allie escapes her ex-boyfriend, who she just broke up with after three years of an off and on relationship. Allie knows she needs a clean break from her ex but it's too fresh for a confrontation so Hannah and Garrett arrange for her to spend the weekend at the boys' place.<br><br>Allie and Dean find themselves alone and one thing leads to another... <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/2HwNnfZ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450627578ra/17449849.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/jYutBIt" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450626824ra/17449794.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Allie's mortified when she wakes up buck naked with Dean beside her in his birthday suit. She doesn't do one-night stands and especially with Dean! While she goes running for the hills, Dean can't seem to shake their night of getting "jiggy" and wants another round. While Dean may be easy going, he's tenacious and gets what he wants. And he wants to fuck Allie.<br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/thescore2_zpsuaufjywp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450627308i/17449828.jpg" alt=" photo thescore2_zpsuaufjywp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Slowly but surely, he breaks her down and I can't fault the poor girl. I was a goner for Dean too even knowing that he doesn't commit, sleeps around and is only good for a good time. Let me tell you, Dean is more than all that and Allie discovers this and then some!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/iCsbC69" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450627342ra/17449834.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And while Allie may not do casual sex and struggles with what exactly she did with Dean and continues to do, she's certainly his match in the bedroom. She's just as adventurous as him...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/RbvizFE" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450627342ra/17449835.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and the intense sexual chemistry between these two was REAL and hot!! <br><a href="http://imgur.com/giQBoBq" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445031593ra/16588975.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In addition to the hot sex, the banter between these two, actually the banter between Dean and anyone was awesome! So funny and witty. And there's this moment with Allie's BOB, Winston, that was just hilarious as well as what ensued after!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/k7GPCCq" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450627342ra/17449836.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The relationship between Allie and Dean was a natural progression and even though there were bumps, all of it was real and nothing was for drama sake. My only complaint and really it's not, is that I didn't want it to end! And Elle leaves us with a real, yummy teaser for the next book about Tuck. I seriously want it NOW!<br> <br>---------------------------------------------<br>Before I sunk my teeth into this delectable book!<br><br><b>Yay! Look what I got on my Kindle!!</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/JE3I1Yc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434159767ra/15180203.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>**ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review.**<br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts.</b><br><br> <a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1477958048" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1477958048" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1477958048?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1477958048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10663845152040575965"><a href='http://amzn.to/1RwteUa' rel='nofollow noopener'>LIVE on Amazon!</a><br/><br/><b>Another absolutely perfect addition the the <i>Off-Campus</i> series! Before I begin I have to say if you haven’t started this series, you absolutely should!</b><br/><br/><i>The Score</i> is Dean’s story and before I even started I had already fallen in love with the rich, college playboy who doesn’t seem to take anything too seriously. But I must say I really fell in love with him when I realized there was more to the fun, easy going guy. Dean may seem aloof, but he is actually very studious, dedicated and </span>
  <span id="freeText10663845152040575965" style="display:none"><a href="http://amzn.to/1RwteUa" rel="nofollow noopener">LIVE on Amazon!</a><br><br><b>Another absolutely perfect addition the the <i>Off-Campus</i> series! Before I begin I have to say if you haven’t started this series, you absolutely should!</b><br><br><i>The Score</i> is Dean’s story and before I even started I had already fallen in love with the rich, college playboy who doesn’t seem to take anything too seriously. But I must say I really fell in love with him when I realized there was more to the fun, easy going guy. Dean may seem aloof, but he is actually very studious, dedicated and caring. <br><br>Allie is Hannah’s bestie and the eternal romantic. She has gone from relationship to relationship, not because she is afraid of being alone, but because she loves being in love. She loves having someone to share her feelings and just the ins and outs of her day. When <i>The Score</i> begins Allie has just broken up with Sean, her off and on boyfriend of three years. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451913918i/17620608._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Allie finds herself with Dean while avoiding Sean, and the two of them end up hooking up. After one super hot, super steamy night Dean isn’t ready to let Allie go. He isn’t looking for love, just a repeat of the best sex of his life, but Allie isn’t into one night stands. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Did you really just take off your shirt?”<br>“Yeah. I don’t like shirts.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Allie and Dean’s dynamic together is perfect. Their relationship is laugh out loud funny, swoon worthy and the perfect amount of sexiness. My favorite thing about Elle Kennedy’s stories is the relationship development and the realness you feel while reading. The teasing and ribbing that goes on between the characters adds a lightness to the story and makes you long to know these guys. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451913918i/17620609._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how Allie, the queen of relationships, tamed the king of the manwhores, Dean. I never expected Allie to be such an adventurous girl, but the fact that she could give Dean a run for his money had me falling in love with her. I love how neither of the main characters were damaged or had some huge thing to overcome. They were both just growing up and developing. Allie and Dean are not perfect and I liked that best of all, it made them more real to me. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451913919i/17620610._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As I said, this series is one of my favorites and to pick a favorite would be like trying to choose my favorite dog. There are parts and characters I like best, but I think Allie and Dean are the best matched. <i>The Score</i> had tons of feels, but it wasn’t too heavy. I was laughing out loud one minute and waiting for the sexy times to pick up again the next. I was swooning over Dean and my heart breaking in the next. I can’t imagine anything I would change about this story, highly recommend!<br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>

<span id="freeTextContainer13494413551995430437"><b>Currently on sale for 99c!</b><br/>*<a href='https://amzn.to/2OAtMcf' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a>*<a href='https://amzn.to/2KU5sQu' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a>*<a href='http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/the-score-elle-kennedy/1122824500;jsessionid=B05B6E953B5AB8E987A9750C5A5E88E2.prodny_store01-atgap04?ean=2940152679663' rel='nofollow noopener'>Barnes & Noble</a>*<br/><br/><b>4 '<i>Stupid Dean and his stupid awesome dick</i>' Stars</b><br/><br/>When Allie breaks up with her boyfriend for the fourth time she vows that it will be the last and that she will stop the cycle of going back to the same man over and over again. Knowing that she won't be strong enough to ignore her ex she goes to her roommates boyfriends place and stays there while the couple is away. But she never expected to walk in on a threesome involving the campus</span>
  <span id="freeText13494413551995430437" style="display:none"><b>Currently on sale for 99c!</b><br>*<a href="https://amzn.to/2OAtMcf" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a>*<a href="https://amzn.to/2KU5sQu" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a>*<a href="http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/the-score-elle-kennedy/1122824500;jsessionid=B05B6E953B5AB8E987A9750C5A5E88E2.prodny_store01-atgap04?ean=2940152679663" rel="nofollow noopener">Barnes &amp; Noble</a>*<br><br><b>4 '<i>Stupid Dean and his stupid awesome dick</i>' Stars</b><br><br>When Allie breaks up with her boyfriend for the fourth time she vows that it will be the last and that she will stop the cycle of going back to the same man over and over again. Knowing that she won't be strong enough to ignore her ex she goes to her roommates boyfriends place and stays there while the couple is away. But she never expected to walk in on a threesome involving the campuses biggest man-slut... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451346781ra/17529807.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dean is the self-proclaimed manwhore on campus and isn't shy at all when it comes to sex. When Allie comes over, interrupting him and two ladies he was having a lot of fun with, he uses the opportunity to get to know her and tries to seduce her. Allie isn't having any of it though, well until Tequila gets involved that is...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451346781ra/17529808.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to admit that I was irrationally upset that Dean wasn't going to be with Sabrina after seeing their fight in <i>The Mistake</i> and getting excited, thinking that they would end up together. <b>But</b> Allie was ten times better than I thought she would turn out to be and I loved her and Dean together.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451346781ra/17529809.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dean is by far <u>my favorite Hero</u> from this series and I just loved how care free he was. Most people saw him as having no responsibilities and as not caring about the important things since he was so laid back about everything but I actually loved that about him. He never let the little things get in his way and he went with the flow instead of worrying about the non important things in life. There is no lie that he is a huge manwhore and Dean is unapologetic about the fact that he loves sex. It was just another thing that made me fall for him and it made him super sexy somehow.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384272739ra/6832990.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Allie wasn't what I expected at all but her character was a good one and I liked seeing her become more confident in herself. Like the typical college student, she was having problems deciding what she should do once she graduates but Dean helped her stop her worrying. I think that's why I liked Dean and Allie together so much, because she grounded him and made him realize his potential while he showed her how freeing it can be to not worry over everything. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451347615ra/17530106.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A lot about this book shocked me and I really didn't expect to have so many emotions while reading. Dean and Allie cracked me up and that scene with the <i>pretty pink vibrator</i> (you'll know the one) is one I will never forget. I was laughing so hard I almost fell off of my bed. When I wasn't crying from laughing so hard I was bawling like a baby at what happened and I still don't think I'm over it. I'm a little mad at Elle for doing that, actually. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389868091ra/8071856.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The reason for my 4 Star rating and not 5 is because after the way the book started, with this huge <b>bang</b> that sucked me in right away, it started to <i>fizzle out</i> and didn't pick up again until around the middle of the book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382070783ra/5640971.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I loved this read and it's my favorite of the series so far. I can't believe it ended that way and now I'm even more excited for whatever Elle has in store for us next. This series has a lot of hype around it which I usually avoid since I end up not liking them as much as everyone thinks I will, but this is the exception and <b>
  <i>I love it</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393489697ra/8721390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Warning:</b> Though there is no cheating or overly descriptive scenes with the H and OW there is talk of his whore-ish ways and not everyone will be comfortable with that. Read at your own risk.<br><br><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1754283172" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8805332316720035698"><b>DNF at 34%</b><br/>UNPOPULAR OPINION ALERT. Also I'll mention porn and sex in a crude way so beware. I recommend not reading this review if you have problem with those topics.<br/>Hell no!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474051370ra/20548158.gif' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This book is not as good as The Deal. It's not as well-written, it's full of filler drama and internal dialogue that doesn't add anything to the plot and the heroine annoyed me so much. She's basically a cheater (she breaks up with Sean and the following night has a one night stand with the hero Dean DeLaurentis), she takes </span>
  <span id="freeText8805332316720035698" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 34%</b><br>UNPOPULAR OPINION ALERT. Also I'll mention porn and sex in a crude way so beware. I recommend not reading this review if you have problem with those topics.<br>Hell no!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474051370ra/20548158.gif" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book is not as good as The Deal. It's not as well-written, it's full of filler drama and internal dialogue that doesn't add anything to the plot and the heroine annoyed me so much. She's basically a cheater (she breaks up with Sean and the following night has a one night stand with the hero Dean DeLaurentis), she takes stupid decisions too often for my taste and as much as I tried to see her ex-boyfriend Sean as the bad guy I couldn't because her attitude annoyed me. And she slut-shamed herself! I really hate slut-shaming.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474051781ra/20548227.gif" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>No, you aren't. But you're disloyal and childish Allie.<br><br>I wanted to slap Allie and talk some sense in her. No honey, no girl should be called slut if she has a one-night stand. I've said this before. Sex is not a sin and a person who sleeps around can be as worthy as someone who doesn't. But how could you feel more guilty for having a one-night stand than for hurting the boy who loved you so much for three years? Someone that didn't cheat on you, that was good for you and for Hannah? Someone you claimed you loved?<br><br>Maybe the ex was mean to Allie in book 2 and deserves to be hurt? I didn't read that book because some reviews of The Mistake weren't encouraging and this one was on sale so I decided to start this one first, but now I regret it. I already returned it and won't continue with the series.<br><br>If there's any woman reading this review who thinks that because some men do this kind of cheating, women should be allowed to do it too, I think you're wrong. This Allie girl seemed to think that she shouldn't apologize to her ex-boyfriend (a man who had been good to her for 3 years) after she sleeps with some one else LESS THAN 24 HRS AFTER THEIR BREAK UP. I hate cheating in romance heroes, but cheating heroines can be equally annoying although I tend to not mind cheating heroines much. The problem is that in this book there's barely any information about Allie in the first 30% other than her inner thoughts about her break up and her monologue about the guilt she feels (for the wrong reasons) after she has one night stand with the hero. It would have helped to see what exactly happened during the break up, because Sean seemed to be under the impression that they'd be back, and although she said she was done, she was extremely hesitant about it.<br><br>Imagine my dear readers that might be reading this review that we're reading a romance in which the couple breaks up and less than 24 hours later the hero sleeps with someone else. You immediately hate that guy, you immediately scream in protest, OH THAT GUY IS A JERK, THAT GUY IS A CHEATER THAT GUY IS ABUSIVE, NEW ADULT PROMOTES ABUSIVE RELATIONSHIPS. BLAH BLAH BLAH.<br><br>But if the cheater is a woman then it's fine?<br><br>Nope not buying it. Cheating is bad and don't tell me it's not cheating just because they were on a break. That argument didn't work for Ross Geller and won't work here either.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474052038ra/20548263.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>The little I saw of Dean in the parts I got to read wasn't particularly good either. It's a very short scene at the beginning were I thought for a moment than instead or reading an erotic romance I was diving into male-oriented porn. There's a difference between porn and erotic romance. Porn seems to be about using and abusing women and honestly makes me want to vomit. Erotic romance is more about the relationship of the MC's and how they fall in love. The first scene of Dean in this book was a threesome with two girls and although it's not a long scene it was more graphic than what my perverted, yet monogamist heart can stand. I don't enjoy reading about lady parts, or about the hero going down on two girl. I don't find girl-on-girl action sexy and I don't want a scene like that shoved into my throat by the author. For a moment I thought I was watching male oriented porn. I also thought for a moment that Elle Kennedy isn't really a woman (of course she is, just a random thought) she was writing that scene as though she was a dude. I avoid porn because I find it yucky. All those women being used, all those fluids and BJ's, all those POV shots that show the human body in a way that it's not pleasant to the eyes. That scene remind me of the few porn videos I've ever seen (out of curiosity and because my male friends told me that it wouldn't be different than reading FSOG) and I didn't like it.<br><br>Dean was a cute, likeable character in the first book of this series. I liked him enough in this book, too.And the twilight talk? GENIUS. That was the part that really made me laugh and make me like Dean a lot. I was slowly falling in love with him, but the heroine disgusted me so much that I didn't want her to be with him, Dean deserves better. That's why I stopped reading. What's the point of continuing if I keep wishing the hero is with someone else? Allie is one of the worst heroines ever. I can't remember when was the last time I read a book in which I got so annoyed with the heroine.<br><br>I think you should give a chance to this book. A lot of people like Dean, the hero, and I can see why. He was funny and caring and I love how concerned he was for Allie.I only didn't finish because I don't want Dean to be with Allie, but if you don't mind cheating heroines or that the couple has sex before we get to know them go for this book. The twilight references made me laugh so much and I know I would have enjoyed it better if I had connected with the heroine.</span>

Holy crap I LOVE HIM, full out <b>AM IN LOVE WITH THE MAN!!</b> He is real right?? It even had my emotions in a tether... Yes I cried too.. Best of the series for me... <br><br>So what can I say to not spoil it for you... These characters are on the kinkier side they both enjoy sex and they happen to get involved in each other at a time Allie needs Dean in her life without her really knowing it. Or to be frank it's what she didn't realise she needed at the time, but boy did the relationship they both fall into be what they both WANT. <br><br>Allie is on rebound from her Ex-boyfriend Sean and Dean is on one hook up to the next. </a><br><br>And then they develop a relationship over time that is gradual and actually develops in a healthy way. What I love about Elle's books are they're fun and heartwarming but you have time to get to know the characters, and by the end I felt like I KNEW THEM. I also was never bored and I jumped in with both feet and kept on till the end... Also I loved that Dean was someone you didn't really know or understand apart from his voyages ways in the other books, he's a MANWHORE and has no Aires or graces about it. Yet in his own book gah I loved his heart, his soul and what was underneath that I never suspected I'd get when seeing him in the others. All I'm saying is he is an open character that had me smiling throughout the whole book. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/F4454F26-6F53-4B93-B959-DB8BB7F8940C_zpsdmhqw0xg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450977727i/17493987._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo F4454F26-6F53-4B93-B959-DB8BB7F8940C_zpsdmhqw0xg.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Allie is likewise a kickass heroine that fought on her own strengths, she's in the acting world so kind of needs to. But on the emotional side she fell for Dean and if there ever were a couple I saw that were a match made in heaven then this couple are it... <br><br>Did I say I love them... 100% swallowed me up!!! <br><br>Fun, sexy, dah-um HOT #PantiesNotRequired HOT and heartwarming... <br><br>That. is. All.. <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/3FB7CFA5-4E02-457B-AE1F-EA443A0CC0EA_zpsbdxcji0k.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436523099ra/15471531.gif" alt=" photo 3FB7CFA5-4E02-457B-AE1F-EA443A0CC0EA_zpsbdxcji0k.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>ARC gifted generously in exchange for an honest review</i> <br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts</b><br><a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9RsFxZcqTAq+H2rWcIL5Wot8QcwQAq8ryftA7BlvOqIXO+fGEvlIQShq93mrRoS/XYbS3F1Zz8QS2rVJvEQv9A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0eeBOVKkLBjPHUiIP/M7gaz7C7eoE8a3H0GtjXZcooUzx2M613coU1lo1SfkN0ZkegGYp+VIpljEYFgo03e30w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
